By Large Ruined House
You stand by a large ruined house in a large clearing which is slowly being reclaimed by the forest vegetation. The upper storey of the house has been set alight recently, causing it to have collapsed. Rubble and burnt rafters block the way to the gaping hole where once stood the doorway that leads East into the house. On the South side of the house there is a walled garden.

> w
You move west.

By Huge Oak Tree
The forest path bends again here, to the East this time around an enormous oak tree with a massive gnarled and buttressed trunk. You can also go NW. Further east you can see what appears to be a large house.

> x tree
A huge oak tree that must be hundreds of years old. The trunk is enormous, over 3 metres across at the base, with gnarled buttresses that rise up from the earth like separate trees that join together to form one gigantic organism. In between two of the buttresses is a small door above which the name "Grimmelmulkinsson" has been carved into the bark of the oak.

> knock on door
You bend down and knock on the small door and call out the name "Grimmelmulkinsson!"

After a second or two a tiny round hatch opens and an eye looks out at you. From the height of the eye above the ground you surmise that the eye belongs to a dwarf.

"Whoever you are, go away!" the owner of the eye shouts at you. "I'm not opening this door until those Xixon reptiles have gone - and the name's 'Grim', not that mouthful!"

The eye continues to stare at you in a fearful and suspicious manner.

(Maybe you could ask the dwarf some questions that will help you find Galhexia?)

> ask about xixon
(Grimmelmulkinsson)

You ask Grim about the Xixon warriors he spoke about.

"There's three Xixon warriors who have set up camp in this part of the forest," the dwarf tells you. "They kill anything that moves and they eat it - even humans and dwarves! One of them tried to sneak up on me and skewer me with a spear! No mate, I ain't opening this door for anyone until they have gone - or are dead!"

> ask for weapon
You ask Grim if he can lend you a weapon you can defend yourself with.

"I only have my sword and I'm keeping that with me," he tells you. "In any case, it is too small for you to use. Sorry I can't help you."
Then Grim spots the catapult you made.

"You've got a pretty effective weapon there," Grim tells you. "All you need do is find a stone and you can do a lot of damage to someone with that catapult!"

> ask about river
(Grimmelmulkinsson)

You ask Grim about the river.

"The river used to be a handy source of fresh fish until that witch arrived," the dwarf tells you. "She destroyed the bridge and turned the fish into carnivores to stop us getting over to 'her' side, but I have a secret way of getting across unharmed."

> show paper to grim
You show the sheet of paper to Grim and ask him if he can read it.

The dwarf's eye scans the paper and it widens in surprise. Grim seems to think for a minute or so then he speaks.

"Yes, of course I can read it," the dwarf tells you, obviously deciding what to ask you for in return. "Bring me the heads of those three Xixons, then I might consider it!"

> ask about secret
(Grimmelmulkinsson)

You ask Grim about his secret way of getting across the river.

"Bring me the heads of those Xixon warriors," the dwarf tells you after a minute or so of thought. "Then I might tell you."

> put paper in bag
You put the sheet of paper inside the canvas bag.

> nw
As you walk northwest from the tree you hear Grim call out.

"OK, bye then!"

Path Bends Here
The forest path that led east from the hedge-lined path bends around to the Southeast here. Above the path looms the trunk of a tree which has fallen over due to the weight of forest vegetation which has choked its branches and it leans against a bigger tree on the other side of the path. You can go West and SE.

> w
You move west.

Path Goes Off East
You are at another junction in the North-South path where a wide path branches off East through the trees. The hedge on the west side is quite high here but you notice it is quite thin and you can see through to the other side.

You hear a noise and look down the path to the south to see two figures, both carrying spears, walking towards you, apparently arguing in a sibilant hissing language - you realise with a shock that they are two of the Xixon warriors that Grim told you about! They are so engrossed in their argument that they have not seen you - maybe it would be wise not to hang around!

> e
You go back along the path the way you came and conceal yourself behind a tree.

You watch as the Xixon warriors appear at the junction where you saw them. Suddenly one of them appears to spot something further up the path from where they are and signals to his companion to stop. He puts his finger against his mouth to indicate that they should be quiet and they both crouch down and ready their spears.

You can only guess that they have spotted a forest animal and are about to try to kill it. Your guess is correct as suddenly one of them throws his spear and they both charge off north along the path.

You wait a minute or two then cautiously walk back to the junction.....

Path Goes Off East
You are at another junction in the North-South path where a wide path branches off East through the trees. The hedge on the west side is quite high here but you notice it is quite thin and you can see through to the other side.

You hear the Xixon warriors shouting in their hissing speech and look north to see them running after something. They change direction to the west and you lose sight of them, but you can still hear them crashing through the undergrowth.

The noise starts to get louder and you realise that they are on the other side of the hedge. You suddenly hear a loud squeal of pain and shortly after two shouts of triumph. Through the hedge you see movement and once again the sibilant sound of the two Xixon lizardmen arguing with each other.

> find stones
You search around on the ground and, choosing some that are as round as possible, you find a handful of stones, picking up as many as you can carry comfortably.

> fire stone at xixon
You fire the stone at the Xixon warriors through the hedge.

Luckily for you, as you release the stone one of the Xixon warriors turns his back on the other and it is this one of the pair that the stone hits on the back of his shoulder.

He turns round in rage and, pulling one of the spears out of the carcass of the boar, thrusts it into the chest of the other Xixon, killing it instantly. The body of the Xixon falls back onto the ground and twitches a few times then lies still. Its killer walks over to the body, kicks it a couple of times to make sure it is dead. You notice he leaves the spear that killed the Xixon in its body.

The remaining Xixon pulls the other spear out of the boar and, bending down to grab the carcass with one hand, hoists it onto his shoulder - you marvel at the sheer strength of these creatures! Pausing only to spit on the body of his dead comrade, the Xixon walks off SW from the clearing and is lost to view amongst the trees.

Path Goes Off East
You are at another junction in the North-South path where a wide path branches off East through the trees. The hedge on the west side is quite high here but you notice it is quite thin and you can see through to the other side.

> w
You push your way through the hedge to the other side.

Clearing in the Forest
You are in a small clearing in the forest on the west side of the hedge that runs alongside the north-south path. All around except for where the hedge is lies thick tangled vegetation that is virtually impassable for a human.  A dead spearman is here.

> pull spear from xixon
You put your foot on the chest of the dead Xixon to hold it down then you pull the spear out. You have to use a bit of effort but eventually it comes out with a sickening squelch and you wipe the green blood off the spearhead on the surrounding vegetation.

> e
You push your way through the hedge to the other side.

Path Goes Off East
You are at another junction in the North-South path where a wide path branches off East through the trees. The hedge on the west side is quite high here but you notice it is quite thin and you can see through to the other side.

> n
You move north.

Path through Forest
You are on the main path which runs North-South through the forest. On the west side of the path bushes and other plants have grown into a tall hedge which extends to the south for some distance. To the NW, past a tree that stands by the path here, you can see another part of the forest path.

> nw
You move northwest.

Bend in Path
You are at a bend in the path where it goes NE and West, although you can see another path to the SE which you can get to by going around the tree that stands at the corner. To the south lies tangled vegetation which grows in profusion around the trees that populate this forest, but to the NW it is somewhat clearer and in a small glade about 7 metres in that direction you see a large clump of tall plants.

You hear a sibilant hiss and look to the NW to see the hidden Xixon archer appear from its hiding place in the clump of bushes and nock an arrow to its bow. The creature pulls the bowstring fully back and aims the arrow directly at you.

> throw spear at xixon

A split second before the archer can loose his arrow, you hurl your spear at the creature. As it releases its arrow it moves to avoid being skewered by the spear, causing the arrow to whizz past your ear into the forest beyond!

The spear hits the Xixon in the upper right of its chest and it screams in pain, dropping its bow and falling back into the clump of bushes from where it had appeared seconds ago. The creature rolls out of the bushes to lie on its back, where it lies there struggling to breathe.

You cautiously approach the wounded creature. It turns its head to look at you and hisses in rage and pain. It reaches up and pulls the spear from its chest and hurls it at you, but its strength is gone and the spear hits your legs side on and clatters to the ground.

Green, ichor-like blood and air bubbling from the hole in its chest, the Xixon tries to stagger to its feet, but the effort is too much for its mortally wounded body and it collapses to the ground and lies still, stone dead!

By Clump of Tall Bushes
You are standing in a small glade in the forest by a clump of tall bushes. You can go either SW or SE back to the path, you are prevented from going in all other directions by the thick vegetation carpeting the forest floor.  Also here is a spear and a bow.  Lying on the ground by the bushes is the body of the Xixon Archer that you killed.

> get spear
Ok, you pick up the spear.

> get quiver
You remove the quiver from the body of the Xixon archer and put the strap over your shoulder.

> get bow
Ok, you pick up the bow.

> se
You move southeast.

Bend in Path

To the south lies tangled vegetation which grows in profusion around the trees that populate this forest, but to the NW it is somewhat clearer and in a small glade about 7 metres in that direction you see a large clump of tall plants.

Path Through Forest
You are on the main path which runs North-South through the forest, about halfway between the path that goes east further North and the bend in the path to the South. On the west side of the path bushes and other plants have grown into a tall hedge which extends to the south for some distance.

> s
You move south.

Path Through Forest
You are on the main path through the forest, where it bends to the SW around the end of the tall hedge and starts to go Downhill. You notice that it is a bit brighter further down, a brightness that extends to the east and west as if there might be a road or a river cutting through the forest. The only other way you can go is North back along the path.

> d
You move down.

By River in Forest
You are standing on the bank of a narrow river in the middle of Direwood Forest. A path slopes up to the NE from the bank here, and you can continue West or East along the river bank here. Further along to the west you can see the remains of a wooden bridge that once spanned the river. Above you the black clouds seem thicker here as they writhe and seethe with malevolent glee.

> e
You move east.

By River in Forest
You are standing on the bank of a narrow river in the middle of Direwood Forest. The bank is quite steep here and the forest vegetation grows very close, so you have to be careful that you do not slip down into the river. The river bends slightly to the SE here or you can go back West. Above you the black clouds seem thicker here as they writhe and seethe with malevolent magic.

> se
You move southeast.

By River in Forest
You seem to be as far as you can go along this section of the river bank, the way further southeast is impassable due to a combination of a nearly vertical bank and the forest vegetation which grows right up to the edge. However, looking Up the slope you notice the vegetation is a bit thinner and you can go that way without ripping yourself to shreds. Otherwise, the only way you can go is NW along the riverbank.  Above you the black clouds seem thicker here as they writhe and seethe with malevolent energies.

> u
You move up.

In Clearing near Dovecote
You are in a long clearing in the forest where a dovecote stands at the other end to the East. You can go Down to the river bank from here but otherwise there are trees and thick vegetation in all other directions.

At the far end of the clearing you see a flash of white against the green background of the forest and look in that direction to see a white dove land on the dovecote.....

In Clearing near Dovecote
You are in a long clearing in the forest where a dovecote stands at the other end to the East. You can go Down to the river bank from here but otherwise there are trees and thick vegetation in all other directions. On the dovecote at the other end of the clearing a white dove is perched, looking warily in your direction.

> get seeds from bag
You take the poppy seeds from the canvas bag.

> throw seeds
You throw the poppy seeds onto the ground in front of the dovecote.

The dove sees the offering and, after a brief check to determine that it isn't a trap, flies down to start feasting on this unexpected meal. As it does so, it lets go of the cotton in its beak, which wafts around in the turbulence caused by the flapping wings of the dove as it lands on the ground.

As the dove starts to peck up the poppy seeds, the cotton floats to earth at the foot of the dovecote. You wait patiently as the dove eats as many seeds as it can find, then it takes wing and flies up to perch in one of the apertures in the dovecote, the ball of cotton forgotten, then it goes inside and is lost to view.....

In Clearing near Dovecote
You are in a long clearing in the forest where a dovecote stands at the other end to the East. You can go Down to the river bank from here but otherwise there are trees and thick vegetation in all other directions.

> e
You move east.

By Dovecote in Clearing
You are at the eastern end of the clearing, where a dovecote stands almost totally engulfed by the encroaching forest vegetation. You can only go West from here, everywhere else is blocked by thick vegetation.   Also here is a tuft of cotton.

As you walk towards the dovecote, you are startled by a loud cawing noise from above you and suddenly you are buffeted by wings as a large bird flies down from its perch in the surrounding trees and lands on the ground in front of the dovecote. It is a magpie.

Cocking its head from side to side as it scrutinises you, the magpie then hops over to the ball of cotton and picks it up in its beak. With a running hop and a skip it then launches itself into the air with a flap of its powerful wings.

You watch as it flies through the largely leafless canopy above and to the west of you and it settles on a branch high up in a tree about 150 metres away. You get a feeling in your gut that the piece of cotton is somehow important, so you had better think of a way to retrieve it from the magpie.

Maybe if you walk around in the forest just to the northwest, you will spot the bird?

Path Through Forest
You are on the main path through the forest, where it bends to the SW around the end of the tall hedge and starts to go Downhill. You notice that it is a bit brighter further down, a brightness that extends to the east and west as if there might be a road or a river cutting through the forest. The only other way you can go is North back along the path.

As you reach the area you think the magpie flew to, you look up and scan the trees for any sign of the bird. Sure enough, you spot it perched on a branch high above you.

> drop all except catapult and stones
Ok, you put down the spear and the bow.

> fire stone at magpie
You place one of the stones in the elastic and grip it with your finger and thumb. You then aim the catapult up at the magpie, pull the elastic as far back as you can and then you release the stone.....

TWANG! The stone zooms up into the canopy towards the magpie and -
THUD! - it hits the underside of the branch that the magpie is perched on and rebounds into the forest undergrowth.

> fire stone at magpie
You fire another stone at the magpie.

You miss the branch and magpie completely and the stone goes flying into the branches above!

> fire stone at magpie
You fire another stone at the magpie.

You miss the branch and magpie completely and the stone goes flying into the branches above!

> fire stone at magpie
You fire another stone at the magpie.

You miss the branch and magpie completely and the stone goes flying into the branches above!

The magpie launches itself off the branch and flies off through the trees to the northwest .

> get all
Ok, you pick up the spear and the bow.

> n
You move north.

East-West Path
You are on a path which runs from East to West in the forest, meandering slightly around the trees. About 7 metres to the NE you see a small glade in which there stands a clump of tall plants.

As you walk along the path looking up into the trees for the magpie, a large dollop of bird poo splatters onto the ground about a metre in front of you. You look up and - as you suspected - you spot the magpie on a branch of a tree directly above the path. You move back a step or two out of the bird's "line-of-fire".

East-West Path
You are on a path which runs from East to West in the forest, meandering slightly around the trees. About 7 metres to the NE you see a small glade in which there stands a clump of tall plants.  Splattered on the ground in the middle of the path is a dollop of bird poo.

The magpie is perched in a tree high above you.

> drop all except catapult and stones
Ok, you put down the spear and the bow.

You miss the branch and magpie completely and the stone goes flying into the branches above!

You miss the branch and magpie completely and the stone goes flying into the branches above!

You just used your last stone. You will need to find some more.

> fire stone at magpie

The magpie takes to the air from the branch and flies off through the trees to the northwest, where it lands on the roof of the abandoned cottage .

> w
You move west.

A Junction of Forest Paths
The path from the East has ended in a junction with another path which runs North - South. Over to the west you can see the shapes of what appear to be small cottages, but you are unable to go directly towards them because of the tangled vegetation hereabouts. Further North, however, you see one of the cottages which lies closer to the path.

> n
You move north.

By Abandoned Cottage
You are standing at the end of the path by an abandoned cottage which is on the west side of the path. In the gloom under the dense forest canopy you see there are other such cottages to the North, NW and NE. The door to the cottage is open and leads In. A thick blanket of leaves covers the path right up to the door of the cottage.  Also here is an old doormat.

You immediately spot the magpie on the roof of the cottage. It stands there, seeming to taunt you by its closeness.

> drop all except catapult and stones
Ok, you put down the spear and the bow.

> fire stone at magpie
You place one of the stones in the elastic and grip it with your finger and thumb. You then aim the catapult at the magpie, pull the elastic as far back as you can and then you release the stone. Surely you cannot miss at this close range?

TWANG! The stone hurtles towards the bird and hits it right on its breast, killing it instantly and hurling the broken body off the cottage roof into the undergrowth beyond. The cotton floats to the ground by the cottage and then you hear the sounds of carnivorous creatures squabbling over the body!

By Abandoned Cottage

In the gloom under the dense forest canopy you see there are other such cottages to the North, NW and NE. The door to the cottage is open and leads In. A thick blanket of leaves covers the path right up to the door of the cottage.  Also here is a spear, an old doormat, a bow and a tuft of cotton.

> get cotton

You put the tuft of cotton inside the canvas bag.

> get all
Ok, you pick up the spear and the bow.  You lift up the doormat, which is heavy with the water that has soaked into it. This movement causes the doormat to disintegrate into lumps of sodden reeds which merge with the leaves lying around you. What was left of the doormat in your hands you toss away.

As you walk south, you see a movement behind a tree to one side of the path. In the gloom you cannot make out what it was but you had better be on your guard.....

N-S Path in Forest
You are on a North-South path in the forest where the trees crowd close together and their branches form a tunnel through which you have to walk. You notice that there are lots of large spider webs festooning the trees and surrounding vegetation in this part of the forest.

Yes, you are certain of it. There is someone - or something - hiding behind a large tree trunk further down the path. Maybe it is the remaining Xixon warrior who killed his comrade earlier on?

You only have a bow and a spear to defend yourself if the Xixon attacks you. Are you brave enough to face the challenge?

> s
You move south.

N-S Path in Forest
You are on a North-South path in the forest where the trees crowd close together and their branches form a tunnel through which you have to walk. All around you large spider webs festoon the trees and surrounding vegetation in this part of the forest.  Also here is a dead spider.

As you approach the tree where the Xixon was hiding, the creature leaps out in front of you, its sword at the ready. Before you can react it swings its sword in an arc intending to lop off your head!

> duck
You duck down and the blade whistles over your head!

You stab out with the spear but the Xixon twists its body and your thrust goes wide. The Xixon swings its sword back to cut your legs from under you!

> jump
You jump into the air, bringing your legs up under your body as high as you can. The Xixon's sword whistles under your feet, missing by millimetres and the Xixon stumbles forward, losing its balance with the impetus of its swing. Its sword flies out of its hand into the undergrowth next to the path, and the lizardman lands sprawling on the path underneath you.

You land on top of the creature with a thump and roll off onto the ground in a heap. You drop everything you are carrying but manage to hold onto your spear and when you look up the Xixon warrior has leapt to its feet and is standing a couple of metres away, weaponless and hissing in rage and frustration!

As you get to your feet the Xixon warrior turns and runs down the path as fast as it can.....

N-S Path in Forest
You are on a North-South path in the forest where the trees crowd close together and their branches form a tunnel through which you have to walk. All around you large spider webs festoon the trees and surrounding vegetation in this part of the forest.  Also here is a dead spider, a catapult, some round stones and a bow.

> throw spear at xixon
You hurl your spear as hard as you can at the back of the fleeing Xixon.....

THUD! The spear hits the Xixon warrior right in the middle of its back. The creature screams sibilantly in pain and throwing its arms out to either side it sprawls forward to land on its face on the path. It writhes around in pain, reaching behind to try to pull the spear from its back, but it is unable to summon the strength. As its life force departs its body, its convulsions cease and it lies still.

> s
You move south.

Sprawled on the path here is the body of the Xixon warrior you killed with your spear.

> get spear
You pull the spear out of the Xixon's back and wipe the spearhead on the vegetation by the side of the path to get the green blood off it.

> s
You move south.

The path bends to the SE just here and starts to slope gently Downwards. The only other way you can go is North back along the path. You notice that there are lots of large spider webs festooning the trees and surrounding vegetation in this part of the forest.  Sprawled on the path here is the body of the Xixon warrior you killed with your spear.

> drop all except sword
Ok, you put down the spear.

> behead xixon
Raising the sword above your head, you bring it down as hard as you can on the dead Xixon's neck!

THUD! The sword slices through scale, flesh and bone as if it were butter and hits the ground under the body. The head rolls away a little way and green ichor-like blood dribbles out of the severed blood vessels in the head and neck.

Bend in Forest Path
The path bends to the SE just here and starts to slope gently Downwards. The only other way you can go is North back along the path. You notice that there are lots of large spider webs festooning the trees and surrounding vegetation in this part of the forest.  Also here is a spear and a grey head.  Sprawled on the path here is the body of the Xixon warrior you killed with your spear.

> get all
Ok, you pick up the spear.  You pick up the grey head, trying not to get any green blood on you.

> get sack from bag
You take the old sack from the canvas bag.

> put head in sack
OK, you put the grey head into the old sack.

> n
You move north.

N-S Path in Forest
You are on a North-South path in the forest where the trees crowd close together and their branches form a tunnel through which you have to walk. All around you large spider webs festoon the trees and surrounding vegetation in this part of the forest.

> n

N-S Path in Forest

> n
You move north.

A Junction of Forest Paths
The path from the East has ended in a junction with another path which runs North - South. Over to the west you can see the shapes of what appear to be small cottages, but you are unable to go directly towards them because of the tangled vegetation hereabouts. Further North, however, you see one of the cottages which lies closer to the path.

You hear roars behind you to the south and you whip around to face that direction, ready to defend yourself. You breathe a brief sigh of relief when you see that the roars come from a pair of large hyena-like creatures which are fighting over the corpse of the Xixon swordsman you killed further down the path.

They roar, snarl and snap at each other for a couple of minutes then one of the creatures backs off. The victor seizes the carcass of the Xixon warrior in its jaws and drags it into the forest, followed closely by the other hyena. You hear the corpse being dragged to the creature's den for a minute or two before the sound of breaking branches and the rustling of bushes fades into the distance.

> e
You move east.

East-West Path
You are on a path which runs from East to West in the forest, meandering slightly around the trees. About 7 metres to the NE you see a small glade in which there stands a clump of tall plants.  Splattered on the ground in the middle of the path is a dollop of bird poo.

The magpie is perched in a tree high above you.

> ne
You move northeast.

By Clump of Tall Bushes
You are standing in a small glade in the forest by a clump of tall bushes. You can go either SW or SE back to the path, you are prevented from going in all other directions by the thick vegetation carpeting the forest floor.  Lying on the ground by the bushes is the body of the Xixon Archer that you killed.

> drop all except sword
Ok, you put down the spear, the catapult, the bow and the old sack.  You drop the round stones on the ground, where they are lost amongst all the other stones around you.

> chop head off

THUD! The sword slices through scale, flesh and bone as if it were butter and hits the ground under the body. The head rolls away a little way and green ichor-like blood dribbles out of the severed blood vessels in the head and neck.

Bend in Path

To the south lies tangled vegetation which grows in profusion around the trees that populate this forest, but to the NW it is somewhat clearer and in a small glade about 7 metres in that direction you see a large clump of tall plants.

> se

Path through Forest
You are on the main path which runs North-South through the forest. On the west side of the path bushes and other plants have grown into a tall hedge which extends to the south for some distance. To the NW, past a tree that stands by the path here, you can see another part of the forest path.

> s
You move south.

Path Goes Off East
You are at another junction in the North-South path where a wide path branches off East through the trees. The hedge on the west side is quite high here but you notice it is quite thin and you can see through to the other side.

> w
You push your way through the hedge to the other side.

Clearing in the Forest
You are in a small clearing in the forest on the west side of the hedge that runs alongside the north-south path. All around except for where the hedge is lies thick tangled vegetation that is virtually impassable for a human.  A dead spearman is here.

> drop all except sword

Path Bends Here
The forest path that led east from the hedge-lined path bends around to the Southeast here. Above the path looms the trunk of a tree which has fallen over due to the weight of forest vegetation which has choked its branches and it leans against a bigger tree on the other side of the path. You can go West and SE.

> se
You move southeast.

By Huge Oak Tree
The forest path bends again here, to the East this time around an enormous oak tree with a massive gnarled and buttressed trunk. You can also go NW. Further east you can see what appears to be a large house.

> knock on door
You bend down and knock on the small door and call out the name "Grim!"

You wait for a minute or so and then the tiny round hatch opens and Grim's eye looks out at you.

"Well! You got rid of those Xixon reptiles yet?" the dwarf demands and his eye glares up at you as he waits for your answer.

> say yes
(to Grimmelmulkinsson)

You tell Grim that the Xixon warriors are all dead, killed by your own hand.

"I will not believe you until I see proof!" the dwarf shouts out at you from behind his door.

> empty sack
You upend the sack and empty the heads out of it onto the ground.....

The dwarf's eye widens and you hear him gasp. "Wow! I don't believe it!" he exclaims in astonishment. "You actually killed them all! Bloody hell...remind me never to upset you, my friend. Hang on a minute and I'll come out."

The dwarf's eye disappears and the tiny hatch closes, then you hear the sound of several bolts being pulled back. An extremely hairy face looks out and peers about to convince himself there is no threat, then the dwarf comes out and stands before you.

By Huge Oak Tree
The forest path bends again here, to the East this time around an enormous oak tree with a massive gnarled and buttressed trunk. You can also go NW. Further east you can see what appears to be a large house.  The dwarf Grimmelmulkinsson is standing here.  Also here is a brown head, a grey head and a green head.

"Ok, I said I would translate that sheet of paper for you?" the dwarf says. "Hand it over."

> get paper
(from the large canvas bag)
You take the sheet of paper from the canvas bag.

> give paper to grim
You hand the sheet of paper to Grim who just gives it a cursory glance. You suspect he already knows what it is and is up to something.

"This is the recipe for Ma Pancott's partridge pie," he tells you. "Mistress Joan's gamebird pies were legendary around these woods before Galhexia came and drove everyone away. You don't mind if I keep this do you, it's of no use to you?"

You say that Grim can keep the recipe, but he must tell you how to get across the river.

"Tell you what," the dwarf says slyly. "You bring me a nice fat partridge so I can try out this recipe and I'll give you what you need to cross the river! Oh, and by the way, I doubt if you have any use for these heads so I'll take them off your hands - they'll make lovely trophies for my collection once I've shrunk them!"

Grim opens the door to his tree house and, kicking one of the heads inside, he picks up the other two and follows the rolling head into his tree and closes the door.

You just stand there dumbfounded, wondering how the dwarf has managed to bamboozle you into doing something for him again!

By Huge Oak Tree
The forest path bends again here, to the East this time around an enormous oak tree with a massive gnarled and buttressed trunk. You can also go NW. Further east you can see what appears to be a large house.

> e
You move east.

By Large Ruined House
You stand by a large ruined house in a large clearing which is slowly being reclaimed by the forest vegetation. The upper storey of the house has been set alight recently, causing it to have collapsed. Rubble and burnt rafters block the way to the gaping hole where once stood the doorway that leads East into the house. On the South side of the house there is a walled garden.

You hear a whirring of wings and a "Kerr-ick" call as a bird is flushed out of the forest undergrowth by an unseen predator. You look up and you see the bird fly over the wall of the garden next to the house and lands somewhere in there.

> s
You move south.

By Archway Into Garden
You are to the south of the house by an archway in the wall which leads East into a garden. The forest has been cleared in this area but the vegetation is growing back with a vengeance.

> e
You move east.

West End of Walled Garden
You are at the west end of a long walled garden by the archway that leads West. The garden is quite long and at the East end you see a potting shed. The forest vegetation has invaded from over the walls and choked everything that was growing here. A partridge is pecking about in the undergrowth under the pear tree at the far end of the garden.

> drop all except bow
Ok, you put down the spear, the catapult, the sword and the old sack.

> fire arrow at partridge
You take an arrow from the quiver, nock it to the bowstring and draw it back. You aim the arrow at the partridge and let go.

TWANG! The shaft arrows towards the body of the partridge but the bird moves slightly and the sharp arrowhead slices through the bird's neck, neatly decapitating it. The body carries on walking for a few steps as if still being controlled by the bird's brain but then it collapses to the ground and lays still.

West End of Walled Garden
You are at the west end of a long walled garden by the archway that leads West. The garden is quite long and at the East end you see a potting shed. The forest vegetation has invaded from over the walls and choked everything that was growing here. The partridge lies dead on the ground at the far end of the garden.   Also here is a spear, a catapult, a sword and an old sack.

> e

You go to walk to the east end of the garden to pick up the partridge you have just killed when from your right you hear a deep growl that makes the hairs on the back of your neck stand on end and you stop dead.

Turning slowly to the right you look up to see a huge wolfhound standing on top of the wall of the garden. The beast bounds down and lops over to the partridge. It sniffs at it then stands guard over it, claiming it as its own. The dog looks directly at you and growls, a deep rumbling sound that comes from its huge muscular chest, as if challenging you to try to get the bird.....

West End of Walled Garden
You are at the west end of a long walled garden by the archway that leads West. The garden is quite long and at the East end you see a potting shed. The forest vegetation has invaded from over the walls and choked everything that was growing here. The partridge lies dead on the ground at the far end of the garden. Standing over the carcass is a huge brindled wolfhound.  Also here is a spear, a catapult, a sword and an old sack.

> get ball from bag
You take the rubber ball from the canvas bag.

> whistle
You whistle at the wolfhound, as if calling the animal to you.

Its head snaps up, its eyes go wide and its ears prick up - it is a long time since anyone whistled at it!

> bounce ball
You bounce the ball on the ground and catch it again.

The wolfhound's eyes go wide as it sees the ball and a plaintive whimper escapes from the animal's mouth as if to say "Please play with me!"

> throw ball over wall
You throw the rubber ball over the wall of the garden into the forest as far as you can.

With a short "Yip!" of joy, the wolfhound leaps up onto the wall and disappears from view in pursuit of the ball, the partridge forgotten!

Also here is a pair of bloomers and a dead grey partridge.

> get partridge

> drop all

> crawl e

Hallway of House
You are in the rubble and rafter choked hallway of the ruined house. A staircase once led up to the first floor, but this has been destroyed by fire. There are doors to the East and South but they are blocked by rubble and debris and impassable. To the North is another hole where the door and doorframe are missing and you can go that way quite easily. The only way out of the house is to crawl under the rubble through the hole where the front door used to be.

> n
You move north.

Burnt-out Room
This room of the house is completely burnt out and you have no idea what purpose it was originally used for. Everything in it has been burned to a cinder and the floor is covered with a layer of ashes and lumps of charred timbers. The hole where the door once stood leads out South to the hallway.

> search ashes
You search the ashes, kicking over lumps of charred rafters. First of all you see ashes and burnt chunks of wood, but then you uncover and pick up a small metal spike.

> put spike in bag
You put the small metal spike inside the canvas bag.

> s
You move south.

> crawl w

By Huge Oak Tree
The forest path bends again here, to the East this time around an enormous oak tree with a massive gnarled and buttressed trunk. You can also go NW. Further east you can see what appears to be a large house.

> knock on door
You bend down and knock on the small door and call out the name "Grim!"

You wait for a minute or so and then the tiny round hatch opens and Grim's eye looks out at you. You show him the dead partridge and his eye goes wide. The tiny hatch is slammed shut and you hear bolts being withdrawn. The door opens and Grim comes out to stand before you. He takes the partridge from you and hands you a small clay pot.

"Pour this potion into the river upstream from where you want to cross and it will scare the fish away," the dwarf tells you. "The effect will only last a few minutes, so if you want to go across then come back again you have got to be quick about it. Don't bother asking for any more, I ain't got enuf to spare."

Grim goes into his tree house and closes the door. You hear the bolts being slammed into position then the hatch opens and he stares out at you.

"Sorry, forgot to thank you for the partridge! I'm going to try Ma Panncott's recipe....I can taste it now!"

The hatch slams shut and you hear the faint sound of Grim singing happily to himself.

> put pot in bag
You put the small clay pot inside the canvas bag.

> nw
You move northwest.

Path Bends Here
The forest path that led east from the hedge-lined path bends around to the Southeast here. You can go West and SE.

> w
You move west.

Path Goes Off East
You are at another junction in the North-South path where a wide path branches off East through the trees. The hedge on the west side is quite high here but you notice it is quite thin and you can see through to the other side.

As you reach the north-south path you hear a loud snuffling snort to your left and turn to see a large boar emerge from the undergrowth a short distance to the south. The huge creature starts rooting around in the pathside vegetation with its nose and long curved tusks, looking for things to eat - you wonder how its skin is not ripped to shreds by the barbs and sharp leaves?

The animal is too intent on its foraging for food to notice you, its eyesight is not very good. However, it won't be long before it catches your scent!

Path Goes Off East
You are at another junction in the North-South path where a wide path branches off East through the trees. The hedge on the west side is quite high here but you notice it is quite thin and you can see through to the other side.  A short distance to the south a large boar is foraging in the undergrowth.

> throw spear at boar
You hurl your spear at the boar with all your strength and score a direct hit in its side and right into the boar's heart, killing it instantly! The creature collapses to the ground and lays still.

> s
You move south.

Path Through Forest
You are on the main path which runs North-South through the forest, about halfway between the path that goes east further North and the bend in the path to the South. On the west side of the path bushes and other plants have grown into a tall hedge which extends to the south for some distance.  Also here is a large, dead boar.

> get spear
(from the large, dead boar)
You pull the spear out of the side of the boar. It takes a bit of effort and you have to twist it a couple of times, but eventually it comes out with a squelch.

You suddenly get that creeping sensation in between your shoulder blades that tells you that you are being watched by someone - or something. You carefully look all around you but see no sign of life. You hope to yourself that there are no more Xixon warriors around!

> s
You move south.

Path Through Forest
You are on the main path through the forest, where it bends to the SW around the end of the tall hedge and starts to go Downhill. You notice that it is a bit brighter further down, a brightness that extends to the east and west as if there might be a road or a river cutting through the forest. The only other way you can go is North back along the path.

You see a movement out of the corner of your eye and you turn to see a large man push his way out of the hedge next to where the carcass of the boar lies on the path. He must have been watching you when you killed the boar - you knew your sixth sense was right!

He bends down and picks the dead boar up as if it were merely a sack of potatoes and slings it over his shoulder. As the man makes the weight of the carcass comfortable on his shoulder he spots you standing there and he looks at you in alarm. The man turns away from you and then sets off at a trot north along the path.

> follow grat
You run as quickly but quietly as you can after the man, keeping him in sight as he jogs along carrying the boar over his shoulder. After a minute he slows down and just walks.

He leads you to the western north-south path in the forest where the spiders webs are and you watch as he turns west from the main path. You hurry down that way and spot a previously unseen track leading west through the thick vegetation, which you follow.

The track leads to a clearing in the forest and you crouch down and watch, concealed by the vegetation either side of you, as the man dumps the carcass of the boar near a large wooden door which is built into an earthen bank which rises sharply on the west side of the clearing.

The man opens the door and goes inside.....

Track through Forest
You are on a well-worn track leading West and NE through the forest. The tangled, impenetrable, shoulder-high vegetation either side of you is so close that your arms brush against it. It is a bit lighter further west, where there is a clearing in the forest.

> get spike from bag
You take the small metal spike from the canvas bag.

The door in the earth bank opens and the man comes out. He walks across to the large hut on the north side of the clearing, opens the door and then goes in, closing the door behind him.

> wait
You wait for a while.....

> w
You move west.

Clearing in Forest
You are in a small clearing in the forest where the trees have been felled and the vegetation completely cut back. The land rises abruptly to the west into a bank over 3 metres high and the trees are much higher in that direction. A painted wooden door, complete with doorframe, has been fitted carefully into the bank to form an entrance to what you assume is a burrow. Over on the North side of the clearing is a tall hut.  Also here is a large, dead boar.

From the hut you hear the man humming tunelessly and loudly to himself. Fortunately the noise he is making drowns out certain other noises that he is making from the other end!

> n
You move north.

By Large Hut
You are standing by the large hut on the north side of the clearing. The door in the bank is to the South. The hut straddles a tiny stream which flows from a spring at the bottom of the earth bank several yards away.

> listen
You put your ear to the door and listen. You can hear a loud tuneless humming but the other noises you hear are not the kind that you like to listen to so you move your head away so that you cannot hear them any more!

> put spike in hasp
You quietly push the clasp over the hasp and slide the spike into the hole in the hasp to secure the hut door closed.

> s
You move south.

Clearing in Forest
You are in a small clearing in the forest where the trees have been felled and the vegetation completely cut back. The land rises abruptly to the west into a bank over 3 metres high and the trees are much higher in that direction. A painted wooden door, complete with doorframe, has been fitted carefully into the bank to form an entrance to what you assume is a burrow. Over on the North side of the clearing is a tall hut.  Also here is a large, dead boar.

You hear the door being pushed open but it is held shut by the spike you put into the hasp. It is pushed a couple more times and you hear a puzzled "Uh! Why door no open?" from inside the hut. The door is then pushed even harder and the clasp is rattled several times as the occupant of the hut realises he has been locked inside.

"GRIM!? Dat you? You shut Grat in hut!?" you hear Grat bellow from inside the hut. "Grat kill Grim when he gets outta dis hut!" he roars, shaking the door so hard that you fear he will get out at any second!

Maybe you should do whatever needs to be done here and get the hell out before Grat manages to get out of the hut!

> open door
You open the wooden door.

> in
You move in.

Burrow Inside Earth Bank
You are standing in a large, man-sized burrow which has been dug out of the earth bank. The burrow has a miscellany of furniture, some of which has been crudely made (such as the single bed and the chair) while other pieces have been salvaged from the ruined house, in particular a desk which is covered by a pile of books. There is a firepit in the middle of the floor with a hole in the roof directly above to take the smoke away. The door leads Out.

The hut door rattles hard and you hear Grat yell, "I get you Grim! You no play jokes on Grat!"

> search books
You search through the books, most of which are of no interest.

Then, at the bottom of the pile, you come across a huge grimoire. You try to pick it up but it is very heavy so you just dust it off - a sixth sense tells you this tome is of great importance!

Burrow Inside Earth Bank
You are standing in a large, man-sized burrow which has been dug out of the earth bank. The burrow has a miscellany of furniture, some of which has been crudely made (such as the single bed and the chair) while other pieces have been salvaged from the ruined house, in particular a desk which is covered by a pile of books. There is a firepit in the middle of the floor with a hole in the roof directly above to take the smoke away. The door leads Out.  Also here is a grimoire.

> read grimoire
You leaf through the grimoire, which has all sorts of spells and recipes for potions, everything from getting rid of warts to love potions. In one section there are some rather dangerous-looking spells, some of which have gruesome results if cast properly, but one spell that particularly catches your eye reads like so:

"To quadruple the effect of any toxic venom so that it will poison and kill instantly even the most powerful of sorcerers, say the incantation 'Nrogara Oblib Fladnag Odorf' over the venom once the venom has been applied to the weapon you are going to use."

You say the incantation to yourself a few times so that you will remember it when you need to.

> put grimoire on desk
You are not carrying nothing!

Grat starts to pound his fists on the hut door and the spike rattles in the hasp - it will surely come loose soon!

Grat yells, "Grat no like it in here, it SMELLS! Please let Grat out, you can have pig....well, half of pig!"

> out
You move out.

Track through Forest
You are on a well-worn track leading West and NE through the forest. The tangled, impenetrable, shoulder-high vegetation either side of you is so close that your arms brush against it. It is a bit lighter further west, where there is a clearing in the forest.

You hear a loud crash as the hut door is finally broken open and Grat comes stomping out in a rage. You crouch down and watch as Grat looks wildly around for the culprit who shut him in the hut, then he runs inside his burrow to search in there.

He comes out a second or two later, realising that you have escaped. He stands there for a minute or two breathing hard while his rage subsides and then, shaking his head and muttering to himself, he goes back inside again. He returns with a huge knife and, crouching down beside the boar, he starts skinning it.

You decide to leave him to it and you quietly set off along the track back to the path in the forest.

All around you large spider webs festoon the trees and surrounding vegetation in this part of the forest.  A barely visible track leads off west through the undergrowth here.

> dip thorn in resin
You dip the blunt end of the thorn into the resin and pull it out again, leaving a blob of sticky glue on the end of the thorn.

You will have to hurry - the resin will set hard very soon!

> stick thorn to cotton
You stick the tuft of cotton onto the blunt end of the thorn to make a dart.

> se

Sure enough, there is a warband of about a dozen Xixon warriors some distance away. They seem to be reluctant to proceed any further along the path towards where you are standing and they gesture to the west as if there is something going on over in that direction that they are afraid of.

> look se

Avenue of Sphinxes

You can see that the sphinxes lead to a circle of massive megaliths above which the black clouds are suffused with lightning and strange bands of glowing fluorescence. Standing guard at either side of the entrance to the circle, some 20 metres away, are two guardians, an ogre and a troll, armed with massive battleaxes. Beyond the guardians you see the sorceress Galhexia in the circle of megaliths.

The ogre spots you and, looking over at the troll, cocks its head towards you. They both heft their battleaxes in their hands, but they make no move to attack...yet!

> cut binding with knife
You cut through the binding holding the spearhead to the shaft. It is very tightly wound and you have to slice along it a couple of times. You throw the bits of binding away, leaving you with a spearhead and a shaft.

> resheath knife
I don't understand what you want to do with the leather sheath.

> remove bag and quiver
Ok, you remove the large canvas bag and the quiver.

> drop all except shaft and dart
Ok, you put down the sheath knife, the catapult, the bow, the quiver, the metal spearhead, the sword, the old sack and the large canvas bag.

> say nrogara oblib fladnag odorf
You say the words of the spell over the poisoned dart. You don't expect anything to happen, as you have never performed magic before, but to your amazement the venom glows a sickly green - it worked!

> put dart in shaft
You push the dart into the end of the tube in the wooden shaft. The dart is now ready to blow at someone or something.

> x tracks
They are from a cloven-hoofed animal such as a boar. You see that they lead into and out of a tunnel which has been made by the animal that left the tracks.

> crawl into tunnel
You lay down on your stomach and crawl into the tunnel.

Tunnel in Vegetation
You are crawling on your stomach in the tunnel through the vegetation. It is big enough for you to crawl through without catching yourself on the barbs and thorns and you can also raise your head to see where you are going. It leads North out to the path and bends SW here to parallel the path.

> crawl sw
You crawl SW along the tunnel.

Tunnel in Vegetation
You are crawling along a tunnel made by an animal in the vegetation. The tunnel passes right next to one of the standing stones that line the avenue just to the northwest. The tunnel continues SW and NE.

> crawl sw
You crawl SW along the tunnel.

Animal Den
You are at the end of the tunnel in the vegetation, which has opened out into a circular den a couple of metres across. The den nestles between the uprights of a megalith on the east side of a huge circle of the stones. You can move around a bit but it is impossible to even sit upright, and any movement sends up a cloud of dust from the nesting materials you lay on. The only way you can go now is to crawl NE back along the tunnel.  Beyond the vegetation and the people gathered within the Great Circle of megaliths, you can see the sorceress Galhexia standing by the altar in the centre.

You look through the thin vegetation between the megalith uprights and realise that you can see directly into the Great Circle - the evil sorceress Galhexia is only about 10 metres away to the west! The circle is crowded with a mixture of people and monsters, all of whom stare trance-like at the sorceress.

You watch, appalled, as a sacrifice is led up to the altar by two demons. The victim, a young man, seems totally oblivious to his impending fate and he meekly lays down on the altar. Galhexia raises a ceremonial knife above her head and chants words that you cannot understand, but which you get the meaning of. She plunges the knife into the chest of the young man and cuts his still beating heart from his chest. Putting down the knife, she takes a glass ball from her robes and holds both it and the heart, dripping with the blood above her head. You realise that the glass ball is the Evil Orb of Allinor that Magor told you about.

Suddenly blue lights begin to flash within the orb and mystic bands of phosphorescence leap out from the orb to form a nimbus around the heart in Galhexia's hand. She throws back her head in ecstasy as the arcane forces crackle down her arms to coalesce around her heart. The demons drag the body away and Galhexia starts to chant once again.

If you are going to do anything about this abomination you had better be quick about it - her minions are standing just metres from you and one of them might spot you!

> x galhexia
A tall, stunningly beautiful woman with long, lustrous black hair, dressed in a scarlet, figure-hugging gown that shows off her figure to full advantage. Knowing that she is Magor's twin sister, however, you realise that the woman's apparent youth is the result of black magic.

> aim blowpipe at galhexia
You lay down and, poking the makeshift blowpipe through the vegetation so that it rests on it and is steady, you aim it directly at Galhexia.

> blow dart at galhexia
You take a deep breath and blow the dart through the blowpipe as hard as you can.

"PHUTT" - The dart flies out of the blowpipe and scores a direct hit in Galhexia's neck. She yells in pain and she staggers back as the venom enters her bloodstream and she falls to the ground on her back. You watch as her body starts to convulse as the ensorcelled venom starts to take effect, but then she rolls over and makes a monumental effort to get to her feet.

Several of her minions rush over to help her, but she pushes them away. Using the altar as support, she manages to stand upright and then she looks around to seek out the location of her assailant. As her head turns in your direction, you see to your horror that her eyes are glowing the sickly green colour of the venom!

The sorceress takes an unsteady step towards you, raising her hand as if she is about to cast a spell at you, but suddenly she throws her head back, her back arches and she screams in agony and rage as the ensorcelled venom finally takes its toll on her body. She gives one last convulsion and then she falls back to lay dead across the altar where she herself had taken so many innocent lives.

All this time, most of the people and monsters in the circle were just standing watching, completely under Galhexia's spell. With her death the spell is broken and there are cries of surprise, bewilderment and horror as they come out of their trance and mill about in confusion looking around at their surroundings, wondering how they got there. Then as people start to recognise friends and family there is much joy.

You crawl back out of the tunnel and as you emerge onto the path you realise that the black clouds that hovered over the forest have dissipated and the sun now shines once again.

Wide Path through Forest
You are on a wide path through the forest, which seems even denser than that on the north side of the river and it is much darker because of the thicker canopy overhead, although further SW the sky is open due to the absence of trees. The path runs NE and SW here and in that direction you see an avenue of sphinxes which seems to lead right into the heart of the forest. Just here you notice some animal tracks in the dirt of the path.  Also here is a sheath knife, a catapult, a bow, a quiver, a metal spearhead, a sword, an old sack and a large canvas bag.

The first things you see as you look around is the ogre and the troll, who were guarding the entrance to the circle of megaliths, walking towards you with a gang of about 20 other monsters from the circle.

For a moment you think to your horror that they are going to take their revenge on you for killing Galhexia, but then to your amazement the troll actually nods at you in greeting and he gestures with his battleaxe at something behind you. You turn to see the Xixon warband you saw on the path over to the east at the bend in the path to the northeast.

As the gang of monsters passes you they break into a run and you watch in surprise as the Xixon warriors turn tail and run for their lives.

The monsters chase after them and you lose sight of the screaming and yelling gang as they charge after the fleeing Xixons.

> get all
Ok, you pick up the sheath knife, the catapult, the bow, the quiver, the metal spearhead, the sword, the old sack and the large canvas bag.

> reassemble spear
You reassemble the spear by tying the spearhead to the wooden shaft with the length of string, passing it through the hole in the spearhead several times and winding the string tightly around both to form a tight fit.

> sw
You move southwest.

Avenue of Sphinxes
You are at the start of an avenue of sphinxes that runs SW from here for some distance towards the heart of the forest. The trees have been felled for about 10 metres either side of the avenue, leaving an area where the evil vegetation and the thorn bushes are dying away, allowing the native flora to re-establish itself. You can see that the sphinxes lead to an ancient circle of massive megaliths above which the black clouds have now dispersed and the sun now shines upon once again.

You meet the first of the people from the circle who are hurrying away from the area as fast as they can go. Some look joyous, but others are distraught on having learnt that their loved ones are dead. As they realise that you are the person who killed the evil Galhexia, you are greeted with handshakes, hugs, kisses and slaps on the back from the grateful folk as they make their way out of the circle.

> sw
You move southwest.

Avenue of Sphinxes
You are about halfway along the avenue of sphinxes that runs SW towards the heart of the forest. Beyond the sphinxes, the forest has been cleared to leave an area where the evil vegetation and the thorn bushes are dying away, allowing the native flora to re-establish itself. You can see that the sphinxes lead to an ancient circle of massive megaliths above which the black clouds have now dispersed and the sun now shines upon once again.

More people pass you as they leave the circle and some stop to greet and thank you for saving them.

One such person is a dwarvish woman who stops to thank you. She mentions that her name is Molka and you realise that she is the wife of the dwarf Grim who helped you get across the river with the potion he gave you. You tell Molka that Grim is alive and well and that he is at home in their tree house making a partridge pie. She cannot believe her ears and, giving you a tight hug which nearly suffocates you, hurries off to be with her beloved husband.

> sw
You move southwest.

End of Avenue of Sphinxes
You are at the end of the avenue of sphinxes where it joins an ancient circle of enormous megaliths. You can go SW into the circle or NE back along the avenue. Beyond the sphinxes and around the Great Circle the forest trees have been felled to leave an area where the evil vegetation and the thorn bushes are dying away, allowing the native flora to re-establish itself.

The last of the people leave the Great Circle. As they pass you some stop to thank you for saving them.

> sw
You move southwest.

The Great Circle
You are standing at the centre of the Great Circle of ancient megaliths. Before you is a huge block of bloodstained stone which has obviously been used as a sacrificial altar. The avenue of sphinxes lies to the NE. The body of the sorceress Galhexia lays sprawled across the altar.

As you approach the altar, behind it the air shimmers and then the sorcerer Magor stands there, looking sadly down at the body of his twin. He shakes his head with sadness and sighs deeply.

"She could so easily have gone on to great things, had she not wanted to retain her youth," he tells you. At your look of surprise he smiles and nods. "Yes, she truly was a woman of great beauty when she was young, as much as I was, ahem, a handsome young man" Magor tells you. "Unfortunately we grew older and while I was prepared to lose my youth and good looks, Galhexia was not. She turned to the dark side of magic to retain her beauty, which sadly corrupted her and lead to her insane and futile search for immortality."

Magor turns and signals to two robed figures who you had not noticed standing in between two of the megaliths. They walk solemnly over to the altar and gently pick up the body of Galhexia. Bowing to Magor, they take a step back and promptly vanish with a "Pop!" of displaced air.

"Evil though she was, she was still my twin sister," Magor explains, "I cannot leave her to rot or be eaten by scavengers. She will be interred in our family tomb with a simple marker.

Magor bends down and picks up an object from where it was lying on the ground on the other side of the altar and shows it to you - it is the Evil Orb of Allinor that Galhexia was using in her rites.

"I will take this and place it where no-one may find it. Never again will it be used for such evil."

Magor disappears from view, but returns a few seconds later, minus the orb.

"The world is safe now that the sorceress is no more," he tells you. "I can now show you the village where King Kolt's tomb is located."

Magor leads you out of the Great Circle and you journey south through the forest, his magic senses steering you clear of Xixon patrols. Eventually you reach the southern edge of the forest, which is on an escarpment overlooking a vast plain.

Southern Edge of Forest
You are on an escarpment overlooking the Plain of Domreil. Behind you to the north lies Direwood forest, the edge of which stretches away to the east and west as far as the eye can see. The land falls away to the south to a vast plain which is dominated by the walled city of Domreil, itself surrounded by the encampment of the Xixon horde which has captured it. The city lies about three or four kilometres to the south and you notice a small village nestling at the foot of the escarpment below you. A wide path leads North back into the forest and you can go Down a narrow trail that snakes down the escarpment towards the village.

Magor points down to the village below.

"This is the village of Espergate that I think my father spoke about," he tells you. "Where Kolt's tomb is or how you get to it I have no idea, I'm afraid. It is up to you to find it. Now, I must depart to supervise the interment of my sister. I wish you all the luck in the world with your quest."

Before he goes, Magor gestures with his hand and the things you left behind are magically restored to you.

"Farewell, Alaric Blackmoon, I must go now as my ability to maintain this spell grows weak," the sorcerer tells you before disappearing with a "Pop!" of displaced air.

> d

THE AXE OF KOLT - Chapter Three:

The Mines of Terror

As you walk along the path that snakes down the escarpment face towards the village of Espergate, you enjoy a brief respite after the horrors of Direwood Forest and revel in the sunshine until you reach the outskirts of the village.

As you approach the village you realise that it is abandoned and that there will probably be nobody there who can help you in your quest. Then you spot the reason that the village is deserted - a Xixon encampment just to the east of the village. This could mean that there might be Xixon warriors in the village itself, so you had better be on your guard.....

Press B then Enter to Begin Chapter 3.....

> b

North of Village
You are on a path which leads South into a small village from the path Up the escarpment. The path joins a wider road here, which has some wagon rails beside it, that heads NW towards the escarpment face. The road and rails continue South through a gap in the buildings while a path leads off SE around the outskirts of the village.

> se
You move southeast.

East of Village
You are on a path on the northeast side of the abandoned village. The path curves around the side of a building here. You can go NW or SE.

As you reach the corner of the building you hear noises coming from the southeast. A sixth sense tells you there might be danger in that direction.

> put lamplighter in pouch
You put the lamplighter in the pouch.

> listen
You stand still and listen carefully. The noises you heard are the sibilant tones of Xixon lizardmen talking amongst themselves. You peep around the corner of the building and see a camp of Xixon warriors to the southeast.

> look around corner
You look around the corner of the building and see a Xixon encampment of about a dozen warriors a short distance south.

> nw
You move northwest.

North of Village
You are on a path which leads South into a small village from the path Up the escarpment. The path joins a wider road here, which has some wagon rails beside it, that heads NW towards the escarpment face. The road and rails continue South through a gap in the buildings while a path leads off SE around the outskirts of the village.

> s
You move south.

As you walk through the village you notice that a lot of the buildings are just empty shells, they never seem to have been occupied. However, others show signs of use and occupation - very strange!

By Corner of Building
You are standing at the corner of a building on the north side of the village square. In the square to the South you see a stone horse trough that the metal tracks go past and beyond that you see a small wagon lying on its side next to the rails. Further to the south beyond the village buildings you see a tall wooden structure. The road between the buildings goes North.

> look e
You look around the corner of the building and see that the east side of the square is open and you see a Xixon encampment of about a dozen warriors about 25 metres to the east. About halfway between here and the Xixon encampment you can see a clump of tall weeds which will hide you from the view of the Xixon warriors if you keep low.

> crawl s
You get down on your stomach and crawl south towards the horse trough, keeping as low as you can so that the weeds hide you from the Xixon warriors.

Behind Horse Trough
You are lying behind a stone horse trough on the north side of the village square, hidden from the view of the Xixon warriors in the encampment on the east side of the village. The overturned wagon is about 15 metres to the south while the building you crawled here from is the same distance north. In the distance to the south you see the tall structure through the gap in the buildings on the south side of the square.

> x trough
A stone trough which used to be kept full of water for horses or pit ponies to drink from. It is carved from local stone and stands on four stubby legs leaving a gap underneath. The water in the trough has long evaporated and there is just dirt and dust inside it now.

> search gap
You search around in the gap under the horse trough. At first all you find is dust, dirt, stones and creepy-crawlies, but then your fingers close upon a small object. You look to see what it is you have found and discover it is a lump of charcoal. You think to yourself that it might be useful, so you put it into the pouch on your belt.

> throw spear south
You throw the spear carefully behind the wagon to the south. Luckily you are not seen by the Xixon and they are not alerted by the sound.

> get catapult
You are already carrying the catapult!

> drop all but catapult and stones
Ok, you put down the bow, the sword and the old sack.

> fire stone over xixon
You fire a stone high into the air so that it arcs over the Xixon encampment and lands far beyond. Luckily it hits a rock and makes a clattering sound that the Xixon warriors hear. They look to the east and a couple of them go off to investigate while the others look on.

> crawl s
You get down on your stomach and crawl south towards the wagon, keeping as low as you can so that the weeds hide you from the Xixon warriors.

Behind Wagon
You are on your knees crouching between the rails and the wheels of the overturned wagon. The horse trough you first hid behind is about 15 metres to the north, while to the south, roughly the same distance away, are the buildings on the south side of the village square with the tall structure beyond.  Also here is a spear.

The Xixon warriors return to their encampment after investigating the noise you caused.

> search rails
Lying right next to one of the rusty rails, almost hidden from view, you find and pick up an old length of fuse. You put it inside your belt pouch for safe-keeping.

> untie string
You untie the string to separate the spearhead from the shaft.

> tie string to spearhead
You poke one end of the length of string into the hole in the end of the metal spearhead and knot it securely.

> spin spearhead
You hold on to the end of the string and start to spin the metal spearhead in a vertical circle at your side. It gets faster and faster until the spearhead is a circular blur.

> let go of string
You let go of the string and the spearhead zooms up into the air in a long arc which takes it high above the Xixon camp to land some distance beyond it. You do not hear the noise it makes but the Xixon warriors obviously did as they all grab their weapons and run off to the east to investigate.

> run s
You get to your feet and sprint from the cover of the wagon towards the buildings on the south side of the square. As the Xixon warriors have left their encampment to investigate the noise you made with the spearhead, you reach the cover of a building safely.

South Side of Square
You are on the south side of the village square, at the corner of a building. The rail track continues south through a wide gap towards a large wooden structure about 100 metres further south beyond the village. To the north is an overturned wagon and beyond that nearer to the north side of the square is a horse trough.

The Xixon warriors once again return to their camp after investigating the noise you caused a second time.

> s
You move south.

South of Village
You are to the south of the village, standing by a tall wooden structure which is the headgear above a mine shaft where the road ends. The wagon rails stop here at a crude buffer beam. The mine shaft itself is covered by wooden boards and you can stand on these if you go South under the headgear. You can also follow the tracks north through the village or go NE around the side of the village.

> s
You move south.

Under Winch Structure
You are standing under the winch structure on the wooden boards covering the mine shaft.

Suddenly you hear a soggy splintering sound as the water-sodden boards beneath your feet give way under your weight and before you can leap to safety you plunge like a stone down into the darkness of the mine shaft.

Yeeeaaagggg! You let out an involuntary yell of shock as you as you tumble head over heels down the mine shaft, dropping everything you were carrying .

Then as you are falling your hand brushes against one of the ropes which hang down the shaft from the winch above.

If you don't do something quickly you are a dead man!

> grab rope
You reach out and grab hold of the ropes as you plunge down the mine shaft. As they are sodden with water your hands are not burnt as you try to slow your fall.

As your speed rapidly decreases you are able to wrap both your arms and your legs around the ropes to further slow your descent.

Eventually you come to a halt and you mutter a heart-felt prayer to whatever gods are listening in thanks for your salvation.

You are hanging on the ropes in the mine shaft in complete and utter darkness. It is completely silent apart from the occasional drip of water down the walls of the shaft, but you can feel a slight current of air flowing past you.

> feel around
Hanging on to the ropes with one hand and both legs you reach out as far as you can. Your questing fingers make contact with the circular wall of the mine shaft and you then turn yourself in a circle to reveal that there are no tunnel openings in this part of the mine shaft.

> climb up rope
You climb up the ropes about five or six metres.

You are hanging on the ropes in the mine shaft in complete and utter darkness. It is completely silent apart from the occasional drip of water down the walls of the shaft, but you can feel a slight current of air flowing past you.

> feel around

Your searching fingers make contact with the circular wall of the mine shaft and you then turn yourself in a circle. After turning for about a third of a circle your fingers meet empty air, indicating that there is tunnel opening on the east side of the mine shaft.

> jump east
You climb up the rope a little more then you swing as much as you can in the direction of the tunnel - which isn't much! As the rope swings towards the tunnel opening you leap out into the void!

You fall towards the tunnel opening and slam into the lower edge. As you scrabble with your arms and legs to get a grip your hand finds a tiny projection in the rock floor which you are able to grab hold of and pull yourself up into the tunnel and safety.

It is completely and utterly dark and you cannot see a thing.

Looks like the only way you can go is East.

You look around at the walls of the storage chamber and see that they are quite rough as this is only a storage chamber. On one wall of the chamber you see a small cupboard.....

Storage Chamber
You are in a large square storage chamber that is crammed with all sorts of dust-covered boxes, crates and rusting equipment. The chamber is about 5 metres square but the ceiling is the same two metre height of the main tunnel, it being supported by a tree trunk! An opening leads out through the western wall to the main tunnel. The floor of the chamber is covered in a layer of thick dust.  On one wall of the chamber is a small cupboard.  Behind the boxes against the wall of the chamber is a rat's nest.

> open cupboard
You pull open the cupboard door, which comes off in your hand and falls to pieces, as does the rest of the cupboard which falls off the wall and disintegrates. The contents of the cupboard fall onto the floor by your boots.

> put bandage in pouch
You put the narrow cloth bandage in the pouch.

> w
You move west.

Main Tunnel
You are in a mine tunnel deep underground which slopes downward slightly towards the south. Either side of you to the North and South you can see the tunnel for only a few metres before it disappears in the fuzzy darkness. On the floor of the tunnel are some wagon rails and in the east side of the tunnel is an opening. You hear a weird moaning sound coming from the south which makes your hair stand on end. You can also feel a strong current of air blowing along the tunnel from that direction.

> n
You move north.

Main Tunnel
