> n
You move north.

Main Tunnel
You are in a circular chamber which marks a crossroads in the mine tunnels, where another tunnel bisects the main tunnel. In the floor of the chamber, which you notice is level, is a turntable on which there are wagon rails running North & South and East & West.  You hear a weird moaning sound coming from the south which makes your hair stand on end. You can also feel a current of air blowing along the tunnel from that direction. It is a bit stronger here and it is blowing along the side tunnels as well.

> x turntable
A round wooden platform about 3 metres in diameter on which there are two sets of rails at right angles to each other. An ore wagon would be pushed or pulled onto the turntable and then it would be turned through 90 degrees so that the wagon was pointing in the new direction that the miners wanted it to go. There are four holes in the edge of the turntable, any one of which would have held a lever to enable the turntable operator to turn it with a fully-laden wagon on it. The turntable is slightly out of alignment and the rails on it are not in line with the ones running along the tunnels.

> push turntable
You push on one of the rails of the turntable to get the ones on it in alignment with the rails leading off along the tunnels. It is a bit stiff from disuse, but you only have to move it a little to get the rails aligned properly.

> w
You move west.

E-W Tunnel
You are in a mine tunnel running from East to West. Either side of you can see the tunnel for only a few metres before it disappears in the fuzzy darkness.  The wagon rails here are intact and straight.  You feel a current of air blowing along the tunnel from the east and an eerie moaning sound coming from that direction as well.

> x tunnel
The mine tunnel is rectangular, about three metres wide and two high. There are support timbers every couple of metres along the tunnel. You notice that the tunnel is almost completely level all the way along.

> drop all except spanners
Ok, you put down the metal saw, the wooden pot, the miner's mallet and the lengths of wood.

> unbolt rail
You find two spanners that fit over the nuts and bolts and put one on the bolt head and the other over one of the nuts securing a section of rail to the next one. You push the spanners in opposite directions and try to unbolt them. You have to apply a lot of pressure but eventually the nut starts to turn and you are able to undo it. You repeat the process with the other three nuts and bolts, and you disconnect a section of rail from the track.....

E-W Tunnel

A section of the wagon rails is missing here where you unbolted and removed it.  You feel a current of air blowing along the tunnel from the east and an eerie moaning sound coming from that direction as well.    Also here is a metal saw, a wooden pot, a miner's mallet, four nuts, four bolts, eight washers, a section of wagon rail and two lengths of wood.

> get all

> drop rail
Ok, you put down the section of wagon rail.

> replace section
First of all you clear the rusty remains and the water-sodden sleepers of the old section of wagon rail away and unbolt the old bolts from the fishplates on the ends of the sections of rails either side of the rusty one.

Next you position the new section of rail in between the existing ones to either side and secure each of the ends of the rails to the fishplates with the bolts using the spanners. It takes you quite a while to do up the nuts, but eventually you tighten up the fourth nut & bolt and the wagon rail track is repaired.

E-W Tunnel

Main Tunnel
You are at the north end of a mine tunnel deep underground which slopes downward slightly towards the south. Just under the roof of the tunnel right next to the mouth there is a metal bar set between two wooden blocks which are cemented into the rock. There is a wagon rail here which runs south along the tunnel. It starts about a metre short of the tunnel mouth where there is a buffer to stop the wagons rolling off the rails into the mine shaft. You hear a weird moaning sound coming from the south which makes your hair stand on end. You can also feel a current of air blowing along the tunnel from that direction.

> saw bar

> saw screws
You saw through the rusty screws holding the wooden buffer, which drops with an echoing thud to the floor of the tunnel.

Main Tunnel
You are at the south end of the mine tunnel where it comes to an end at an opening. Beyond this is a gigantic fissure in the rock, lit by a strange bio-luminescence which is enhanced by your goggles so that you can see the mouth of another tunnel on the opposite side, which you judge is about 10 metres away. The wagon rails end here where they have broken off because the bridge that once supported them across the fissure has fallen away. The floor of the tunnel slopes slightly upwards to the north. The rails have also been levered over towards the east side of the tunnel.

The eerie moaning noise you heard from further up the tunnel is actually the sound of a fierce wind that blows from east to west along the fissure, and which also blows along the tunnel.

> drop buffer
Ok, you put down the wooden buffer.

> look along rails
You crouch down and look along the line of the wagon rails to see where they point to. You see that the rails lie flat on the tunnel floor and point directly at the end of the rails in the tunnel on the other side of the fissure.

> slide buffer under rails
Using the metal bar to lever the rails up, you push the buffer underneath the rails with your foot so that the rails form a ramp.

> lever rails west
You lever the rails about 10 cm over to the west side of the tunnel using the bar.

> look along rails
You crouch down and look along the line of the wagon rails to see where they point to. You see that the rails are raised up by the buffer beam to form a ramp and point slightly to the right (or west) of the rails in the tunnel on the other side of the fissure.

Just under the roof of the tunnel right next to the mouth there are two wooden blocks set into the rock which used to have the metal bar between them. The wagon rail stops about a metre short of the tunnel mouth, there are two uprights which used to support a buffer beam here. You can feel and hear the wind blowing from the fissure at the south end of the tunnel.  Also here is an ore wagon and a metal saw.

> put pin in lug
You insert the metal pin into the holes in the metal lugs to stop the ore container from swivelling.

> put bar in brake
You put the metal bar into the tube behind the brake to form a brake lever.

> s

You move south.

Main Tunnel
You are in a mine tunnel deep underground which slopes downward slightly towards the south. Either side of you to the North and South you can see the tunnel for only a few metres before it disappears in the fuzzy darkness. On the floor of the tunnel are some wagon rails. You can feel and hear the wind blowing from the fissure at the south end of the tunnel.

> s
You move south.

Main Tunnel

Main Tunnel
You are in a circular chamber which marks a crossroads in the mine tunnels, where another tunnel bisects the main tunnel. In the floor of the chamber, which you notice is level, is a turntable on which there are wagon rails running North & South and East & West.  You can feel and hear the wind blowing from the fissure at the south end of the tunnel.

> w
You move west.

E-W Tunnel
You are in a mine tunnel running from East to West. Either side of you can see the tunnel for only a few metres before it disappears in the fuzzy darkness.  A section of the wagon rails is missing here where you unbolted and removed it.  You hear and feel the wind from the fissure blowing along the tunnel from the east.

> w
You move west.

E-W Tunnel
You are in a mine tunnel running from East to West. Either side of you can see the tunnel for only a few metres before it disappears in the fuzzy darkness.  You feel a current of air blowing along the tunnel from the east and an eerie moaning sound coming from that direction as well.

> w
You move west.

E-W Tunnel
You are nearly as far as you can go at this end of the tunnel. It continues west for a short distance but you can see that there has been a rock fall further along. A pit prop on one side of the tunnel has fallen down and the roof support beam has fallen down on that side so that one end is resting on the pit prop, which lies across the rails on the floor of the tunnel. You hear and feel the wind from the fissure blowing along the tunnel from the east.

> carefully move beam
You very carefully lift the end of the roof support beam off the pit prop and stop for a few seconds. No bits of rock or dust fall from the tunnel roof, so then you slowly swing the beam towards the end of the tunnel until it is clear of the pit prop. Holding your breath, you gently lower the end of the support beam down onto the floor of the tunnel. One or two tiny bits of rock fall from the roof and you stand still for what seems like an eternity before letting out your breath from your tortured lungs and sighing deeply with relief.

E-W Tunnel
You are nearly as far as you can go at this end of the tunnel. It continues west for a short distance but you can see that there has been a rock fall further along. A pit prop on one side of the tunnel is missing and the roof support beam has fallen down on that side so that one end is resting on the floor of the tunnel. You hear and feel the wind from the fissure blowing along the tunnel from the east.  Also here is a pit prop.

> get prop
OK, you pick up the pit prop.

> e
You move east.

Main Tunnel
You are at the north end of a mine tunnel deep underground which slopes downward slightly towards the south. Just under the roof of the tunnel right next to the mouth there are two wooden blocks set into the rock which used to have the metal bar between them. The wagon rail stops about a metre short of the tunnel mouth, there are two uprights which used to support a buffer beam here. You can feel and hear the wind blowing from the fissure at the south end of the tunnel.  Also here is an ore wagon and a metal saw.

> put prop in wagon
You reach up and put the pit prop into the ore wagon.

> climb in wagon
You clamber up into the ore wagon.

In Ore Wagon
You are kneeling inside the cargo compartment of the ore wagon. You are unable to stand up straight as the roof of the mine tunnel is only about half a metre above the top of the wagon. You can see the end of the brake lever sticking up above the side of the wagon. The wagon is currently facing in a north and south direction.  Also here is a miner's mallet, a pit prop and two lengths of wood.

> push roof n
You push the tunnel roof to the north and get the wagon moving.....

As the tunnel slopes down to the south, the wagon starts to pick up speed as it trundles down the wagon rails.....

Press Any Key....
You are jostled about in the wagon as it careers over the turntable, the metallic rumble of the wheels echoing around the circular chamber as it hurtles into the southern section of the tunnel.....

Press Any Key....
You look over the top of the ore compartment and see the support beams on the tunnel roof and walls flashing past at an increasing rate and then out of the fuzzy gloom through the goggles you see the mouth of the tunnel approaching fast.....

Press Any Key....
WWWHHHOOOSSSHHH!!! The wagon zooms into the fissure! The fierce wind blows it in an easterly direction just enough to send the wagon slightly off course!

The wagon's flight across the fissure lasts just a second or two before the wheels land on the rails in the tunnel with a screech of tortured metal. The wagon's momentum almost causes it to tip over, but you throw yourself over to the other side of the ore container and the other two wheels make contact with the rails!

Press Any Key....
The wagon is careering along the tunnel at an incredible speed!

> pull brake
You grab hold of the brake lever and pull back on it with all of your strength, pushing against the front of the ore container with your foot to give you extra leverage. The careering wagon starts to slow down and you hang on for dear life as it comes to a stop. You let go of the brake lever and fall to the floor of the wagon in relief - you made it across the fissure!

> get prop
OK, you pick up the pit prop.

> throw prop out of wagon
The pit prop lands on the floor of the tunnel by the wagon.

> get all
Ok, you pick up the miner's mallet and the lengths of wood.

> throw all out of wagon
OK, everything you were carrying lands on the floor of the mine tunnel by the wagon.

> climb out of wagon
You climb out of the ore wagon into the mine tunnel.

South Tunnel
You are in a mine tunnel deep underground. Either side of you to the North and South you can see the tunnel for only a few metres before it disappears in the fuzzy darkness. On the floor of the tunnel are some wagon rails. The wind from the fissure has died to no more than a breeze.  Also here is an ore wagon, a miner's mallet, a pit prop and two lengths of wood.

> get all
You cannot pick up the ore wagon, it is far too heavy!  Ok, you pick up the miner's mallet and the lengths of wood.  You are carrying too much, you will have to drop everything you are carrying before you can pick up the pit prop.

> s
You move south.

South Tunnel
You are in a mine tunnel deep underground. Either side of you to the North and South you can see the tunnel for only a few metres before it disappears in the fuzzy darkness. On the floor of the tunnel are some wagon rails. The breeze from the fissure is hardly noticeable here. One of the support timbers on the east side of the tunnel is split and looks as if it might collapse.

As you look around you become aware of another noise coming from the south. You look in that direction and can just about make out a fuzzy glow some distance away in the darkness. You hear the noise again - which sounds like something being tapped against rock.

> s
You move south.

South Tunnel
You are in a mine tunnel deep underground. Either side of you to the North and South you can see the tunnel for only a few metres before it disappears in the fuzzy darkness. On the floor of the tunnel are some wagon rails. The air is strangely still here, you cannot feel the wind from the fissure at all, although you can still just about hear the noise it is making.  A few metres to the south you see a ghostly apparition.

The apparition, which is a Tunnel Wight, is tapping the rock wall with a chisel and listening carefully to the sound the chisel makes.

> remove talisman
OK, you remove the talisman from around your neck.

The apparition becomes aware of your presence, stops tapping the wall and turns to face you. Its eyes glow with a mystic green light and you feel a curious languor seep into your lower limbs.

> show talisman
You hold the talisman up so that it is visible to the Tunnel Wight.

The apparition starts to walk towards you, its eyes fixed upon you and arms outstretched in front of it.

> say dispellarius lombardo
(to ghostly apparition)

You say the words "Dispellarius Lombardo" and the apparition stops dead, its ghostly fingers just centimetres from your chest. You hear a loud echoing sigh and the apparition starts to fade away. As the feeling of languor washes from your legs the apparition drops the chisel, which falls to the floor with an echoing clatter, raises a hand in farewell and you feel a deep sense of relief as it finally disappears from view.

South Tunnel
You are in a mine tunnel deep underground. Either side of you to the North and South you can see the tunnel for only a few metres before it disappears in the fuzzy darkness. On the floor of the tunnel are some wagon rails. The air is strangely still here, you cannot feel the wind from the fissure at all, although you can still just about hear the noise it is making.  Also here is a metal chisel.

Now it has served its purpose, you put the talisman back around your neck.

> get chisel
Ok, you pick up the metal chisel.

> s
You move south.

South Tunnel
You are at the south end of the mine tunnel where it ends in a rough rock wall. The wagon rails stop here but there is no buffer beam like there was at the end of the northern section across the fissure. There is no wind here at all and the noise it makes is just a ghostly whisper.

> x rough wall
This wall is where the miners were last working in this tunnel. You have no idea why they stopped mining, maybe the ore they were excavating ran out? In the rough wall at the end of the tunnel you spot a small hole with something inside it.

South Tunnel
You are at the south end of the mine tunnel where it ends in a rough rock wall. The wagon rails stop here but there is no buffer beam like there was at the end of the northern section across the fissure. There is no wind here at all and the noise it makes is just a ghostly whisper.  In the middle of the rock wall at the end of the tunnel you see a small hole with the end of a stick of explosive sticking out of it.

> get explosive
Ok, you take the stick of explosive out of the hole.

> get all from pouch
You take the lamplighter, the short length of fuse and the narrow cloth bandage from the leather pouch.

> fit fuse to explosive
You push one end of the length of fuse into the end of the stick of explosive. It is now ready for use.

> n
You move north.

South Tunnel

On the floor of the tunnel are some wagon rails. The air is strangely still here, you cannot feel the wind from the fissure at all, although you can still just about hear the noise it is making.

South Tunnel
You are in a mine tunnel deep underground. Either side of you to the North and South you can see the tunnel for only a few metres before it disappears in the fuzzy darkness. On the floor of the tunnel are some wagon rails. The breeze from the fissure is hardly noticeable here. One of the support timbers on the east side of the tunnel is split and looks as if it might collapse.

> tap east wall
You tap on the eastern wall of the mine tunnel with the chisel. The noise the rock makes sounds hollow - there might be a cave or some other empty space on the other side of the rock wall.

> drop all except chisel and mallet
Ok, you put down the lamplighter, the stick of explosive, the narrow cloth bandage and the lengths of wood.

> make hole in east wall
Using the mallet and chisel you make a hole in the east wall of the tunnel deep enough to take the stick of explosive. It takes you quite a while and it is noisy and exhausting work. As you hit the chisel one last time you hear it snap and as you pull it out of the hole you have made you see that the tip has broken off.

South Tunnel

South Tunnel
You are in a mine tunnel deep underground. Either side of you to the North and South you can see the tunnel for only a few metres before it disappears in the fuzzy darkness. On the floor of the tunnel are some wagon rails. The breeze from the fissure is hardly noticeable here. There is a small hole in the east wall of the tunnel. Protruding from the hole is the stick of explosive. One of the support timbers on the east side of the tunnel is split and looks as if it might collapse.  Also here is a lamplighter, a miner's mallet, a narrow cloth bandage, two lengths of wood and a broken metal chisel.

> x tunnel
The mine tunnel is rectangular, about three metres wide and two high. There are support timbers every couple of metres along the tunnel. You notice that the tunnel is almost completely level all the way along.

> x timbers
Two uprights either side of the tunnel supporting a beam under the roof.  The upright support timber against the eastern wall is split and looks as if it might collapse.

> prop roof with prop
You place the pit prop under the roof beam, pushing it against the weakened one as far as you can.

> get all
Ok, you pick up the lamplighter, the miner's mallet, the narrow cloth bandage, the lengths of wood and the broken metal chisel.

> hammer prop with mallet
You hammer the bottom end of the prop with the mallet to wedge it firmly under the roof beam.

> light fuse
You try to light the end of the fuse with the lamplighter. The fuse refuses to ignite at first, but then after four or five tries the fuse bursts into flame and starts to burn and fizz, dazzling you slightly through the goggles.

Now the fuse is burning you had better get clear and prepare yourself for a big bang!

> put lamplighter in pouch
You put the lamplighter in the pouch.

> n
You move north.

South Tunnel
You are in a mine tunnel deep underground. Either side of you to the North and South you can see the tunnel for only a few metres before it disappears in the fuzzy darkness. On the floor of the tunnel are some wagon rails. The wind from the fissure has died to no more than a breeze.  Also here is an ore wagon.

> n
You move north.

South Tunnel
You are in a mine tunnel deep underground. Either side of you to the North and South you can see the tunnel for only a few metres before it disappears in the fuzzy darkness. On the floor of the tunnel are some wagon rails. On the west side of the tunnel here is a small alcove. The wind from the fissure blows along the tunnel but it is no more than a light breeze here.

The explosive will detonate at any second!

> w
You move west.

Alcove
You are in a narrow alcove in the rock. It is about a metre and a half deep and about a metre wide.  Also here is a human skeleton, a pickaxe and a shovel.

> wrap bandage around ears
You wind the cloth bandage around your head so that it covers your ears.

B - O - O - O - M!

The explosive detonates, blowing a hole in the wall of the tunnel. A cloud of dust, stones and lumps of rock are hurled along the tunnel, but you are protected from those in the alcove. The loud detonation hits you like a hammer-blow, but your ears are protected as you had covered them.

You stay in the alcove for quite a while until the dust has settled and then you unwrap the bandage from around your ears.

Alcove
You are in a narrow alcove in the rock. It is about a metre and a half deep and about a metre wide.  Also here is a human skeleton, a pickaxe and a shovel.

> get all
You think about picking up the skeleton but decide to leave it where it was as a mark of respect.  Ok, you pick up the pickaxe and the shovel.

> put bandage in pouch
You put the narrow cloth bandage in the pouch.

> e
You move east.

South Tunnel
You are in a mine tunnel deep underground. Either side of you to the North and South you can see the tunnel for only a few metres before it disappears in the fuzzy darkness. South Tunnel

South Tunnel
You are in a mine tunnel deep underground. Either side of you to the North and South you can see the tunnel for only a few metres before it disappears in the fuzzy darkness. On the floor of the tunnel are some wagon rails. The breeze from the fissure is hardly noticeable here. The roof support beam here has been strengthened by the addition of another pit prop. Right next to the support timbers is a big hole in the east wall of the tunnel.

> throw all through hole
You throw everything you are carrying through the hole in the tunnel wall into the cave beyond.

> climb into cave
You climb into the hole and down to the cave beyond.

A Rock-Strewn Crevice
You are in a narrow rock-strewn crevice, the smooth uneven walls and floor of which suggest that this is a natural cavity in the rock rather than a man-made one. The crevice is only about a metre or so wide at its widest point near the hole you blew in the tunnel wall and narrows to an opening about half a metre wide to the SE. Looking up you cannot see any roof, but a trickle of water flows down the walls from the SE to exit via a narrow crack in the northwest corner of the cave. The floor is strewn with lumps of rock from the explosion, so you had better watch your step. The only other exit from the cave is through the hole back into the mine tunnel.  Also here is a miner's mallet, a pickaxe, a shovel, two lengths of wood and a broken metal chisel.

> get all
Ok, you pick up the miner's mallet, the pickaxe, the shovel, the lengths of wood and the broken metal chisel.  The lumps of rock are of no use to you whatsoever.

> se
You leave the cave and find yourself in a narrow fissure in the rock which twists and turns as it slopes upwards towards the southeast. The water trickling along the floor and the smoothness of the walls tell you that the fissure has been widened over the millennia by the action of the water flowing through it. After only a few minutes of picking your way through the darkness you reach a dead end.

A Dead End
You are at a dead end in the underground passageway, in a roughly oblong chamber in the rock. The water that flows under your feet comes through a narrow crack at the top of the southern wall. The only way you can go is to the West back along the fissure to the cave where you broke through from the mine tunnel.

Suddenly you hear the sound of a sinuous body slithering over the rocks and turn to see a snake gliding towards you, its mouth open and fangs deployed ready to bite you!

You leap back and - grabbing a rock from the floor - smash it down on the serpent's head! You fail to kill it but it is mortally injured and squirms away into the darkness whence it came. You breath a sigh of relief at your close call and hurl the rock in the direction that the snake disappeared.

> tap east wall
You tap the east wall and the hollow thud tells you that the rock sounds very thin.

> drop all except pickaxe
Ok, you put down the miner's mallet, the shovel, the lengths of wood and the broken metal chisel.

> demolish east wall with pickaxe
You hit the wall of the cave with the pickaxe and to your astonishment it goes right through the rock - the wall must be very thin! You attack the rock with renewed vigour and within a few minutes you have completely demolished the wall, which you see leads to what seems to be yet another tunnel.

A Dead End
You are at the end of the fissure where you have demolished the east wall. You can either go West back along the fissure to the cave where you broke through from the mine tunnel or you can go East into the passageway beyond.  Also here is a miner's mallet, a shovel, two lengths of wood and a broken metal chisel.

> get all
Ok, you pick up the miner's mallet, the shovel, the lengths of wood and the broken metal chisel.

> e
You move east.

In Tomb Passageway
You are near the south end of a long passageway that slopes down to the North and up towards the South. The floor and ceiling are formed from slabs of stone and the walls, which are white with various scenes painted on them, are lined with bricks. There is a hole in the west wall where you broke through from the dead end.

Your heart skips a beat as you see the paintings on the wall of the passageway and you realise that you have found the entrance to Kolt's tomb!

Then you remember Magor's warning that there may be traps here - you had better be on your guard!

> s
You move south.

South End of Passageway
You are at the south end of a long underground passageway which slopes down towards the North. The passage floor and ceiling are formed from stone slabs and the east, west and south walls are made of white-painted brick.  Painted on the walls are scenes from the early life of King Kolt.

> drop all except pickaxe
Ok, you put down the miner's mallet, the shovel, the lengths of wood and the broken metal chisel.

> demolish south wall with pickaxe
You hit the brick wall with the pickaxe and prise loose one of the bricks. Behind the wall there is what looks like a wall of earth. You hit the wall again and again, eventually bringing the whole wall down to reveal the wall of hard packed earth.

South End of Passageway
You are at the south end of a long underground passageway which slopes down towards the North. The passage floor and ceiling are formed from stone slabs and the east and west walls are made of white-painted brick, while the south wall has been demolished to reveal a wall of earth.  Painted on the walls are scenes from the early life of King Kolt.  Also here is a miner's mallet, a shovel, two lengths of wood, a pile of bricks and a broken metal chisel.

> get wood
Ok, you pick up the lengths of wood.

> n
You move north.

In Tomb Passageway
You are near the south end of a long passageway that slopes down to the North and up towards the South. The floor and ceiling are formed from slabs of stone and the walls, which are white with various scenes painted on them, are lined with bricks. There is a hole in the west wall where you broke through from the dead end.

> n
You move north.

Middle of Passageway
You are roughly at the middle of the passageway, which slopes down to the North, both ends being invisible to you through the goggles. The floor and ceiling are formed from slabs of stone and the walls, which are white with various scenes painted on them, are lined with bricks.

> n

You move north.

As you walk along the passageway, you suddenly experience a strong sense of impending danger and so you stop in order to look for whatever might be the cause.

Tomb Passageway
You are in an underground passageway that slopes down towards the north and up towards the south. The floor and ceiling are formed from slabs of stone and the walls, which are white with various scenes painted on them, are lined with bricks.

> x walls
You notice a line of small holes in the walls at about waist height, they start a couple of steps further along the passageway. You also notice that some of the floor slabs ahead of you stand slightly proud of the others. You suspect that if you step onto the floor ahead, arrows would be fired from the holes.

> x holes
A line of about a dozen holes in each wall of the passageway at about waist height.

> throw pickaxe on floor
You throw the pickaxe onto the floor of the passageway ahead of you.

It lands heavily on the floor and there is a loud click as a trigger is tripped and you jump back as crossbow bolts are fired in various directions from each of the holes along the walls! They hit the walls, floor and ceiling of the passageway with tremendous force and many of them shatter into pieces with the impact.

You realise that even if you had crawled along the floor under the line of holes, you would still have been hit - and probably killed or at least badly wounded - by at least 3 or 4 of the bolts which were fired at the floor.

> n
You move north.

Tomb Passageway
You are in a section of the tomb passageway with holes in the walls at waist height either side of you. You can go North or South. The floor and ceiling are formed from slabs of stone and the walls, which are white with various scenes painted on them, are lined with bricks.  In the walls on either side there are a line of holes at about waist height.  A couple of dozen crossbow bolts lie around on the floor.  Also here is a pickaxe.

> n
You move north.

Near North End of Passageway
You are near the north end of the passageway leading to Kolt's tomb. The floor levels out here and you can see that the passageway ends a bit further north at double bronze doors which are closed. To the south is the area where there are holes in the walls.

> x ceiling
You look up at the ceiling of the passageway and you notice that the slab of stone nearest to the bronze doors has a small gap all the way around it.

> get bandage
(from the leather pouch)
You take the narrow cloth bandage from the leather pouch.

> tie wood together
You put the two pieces of wood together with the ends overlapping and you bind them tightly with the bandage to form one long piece of wood.

> push doors open with wood
You reach out with the long piece of wood and push the bronze doors open. They swing open as they are not locked and as they do so you hear a loud click.....

The slab of stone directly above the doors suddenly drops down from the ceiling, ripping the wood out of your hand as you jump back to avoid getting crushed! The block of stone hits the floor of the passageway with an enormous crash which echoes deafeningly off the walls.

Near North End of Passageway
You are near the north end of the passageway leading to Kolt's tomb. The floor levels out here and you can see that the passageway ends a bit further north at double bronze doors which are open. To the south is the area where there are holes in the walls. Ahead of you lies a massive slab of stone which dropped from the ceiling when you opened the bronze doors.

> n
You move north, squeezing past the block of stone.

North End of Passageway
You are at the north end of the passageway, on the north side of the stone slab that fell from the ceiling when you pushed the bronze doors open. The doors are open and lead North into an antechamber.

> n
You move north.

South End of Antechamber
You are just inside the south end of a small antechamber between the bronze doors which are open and some gold doors which are closed. Beyond the bronze doors a massive slab of stone lies on the floor after dropping from the ceiling when you opened the doors.

As you enter this small room, which is completely and bare except for the doors at either end, you wonder what its purpose was? Then it occurs to you that there might be another trap here!

> x floor slabs
You notice a narrow gap running around the edge of the slabs near the edges of the antechamber, with another similar gap running north-south down the middle.

You realise that there is a false floor ahead of you and if you step onto it a trapdoor will open, plunging you into into a death trap!

> close doors
You close the bronze doors.

> walk around edge
With your back to the wall, you edge around the narrow strip of solid floor around the trapdoor to the north side of the antechamber.

North End of Antechamber
You are standing on the narrow edge of floor at the north end of the small antechamber. In front of you there are some golden doors which are closed. The bronze doors at the south end of the antechamber are also closed.

> open doors
You open the gold doors.

> n
You move north.

Kolt's Tomb
You are in the tomb of King Kolt. It is surprisingly small, only about 4 metres square. The walls, floor and ceiling are lined with marble. The only exit is South.  On a dais on the north side of the room is a large golden throne.  Sitting on the throne is the figure of King Kolt.

> x kolt
King Kolt was a tall, muscular man with a regal bearing when he was alive. His body, dessicated by time, sits upright on his throne, his hands clenched around the shaft of his legendary axe. He still wears his royal regalia and a small crown upon his head.

> get axe
You reach out and try to take the Axe of Kolt from the king's hands.....

A gasp of astonishment escapes your mouth as the long-dead king's eyes snap open and his grip on the axe seems to strengthen!

His eyes glow a bloody red for a second or two and his features seem to relax as you grip the shaft of the axe. You feel an odd sensation in your hand which starts to spread along your arm, manifesting in a deep sense of peace and well-being which suffuses your whole body and you feel quite a bit stronger.

A smile seems to flicker across Kolt's face as his grip on the axe slackens and you are able to lift it off his thighs. You step back in surprise as his body suddenly collapses in on itself and everything, including his clothes, crumbles into dust!

A strong breeze mysteriously swirls around the room, the dust left from Kolt's body twisting upwards to disappear as it hits the ceiling. You are startled out of your wits as the king's crown hits the throne and rolls off to clatter on the floor, the only thing left of the king apart from the Axe of Kolt in your hands.

THE AXE OF KOLT - Chapter Four:

Fortress of the Xixon

You endure a slow, bone-rattling journey in the wagon until you reach Domreil. From your cramped position on the floor of the wagon, you look up beyond the figures of the Xixon guards surrounding you to see the city walls looming up. Then you pass under the outer gate, through the town that surrounds the castle and then through the massive curtain inner walls into the castle itself.

The wagon comes to a halt and couple of your guards lift you effortlessly out of the wagon and you are dragged along dark corridors and down into the castle dungeons where you are dumped on the floor.....

Press B then Enter to Begin Chapter 4.....

> b

The Castle Dungeons (Lying on floor)
You are lying on the damp, slimy floor of the castle dungeons, your hands and feet are bound tightly. You are surrounded by several Xixon warriors who would prevent your escape even if you could get free of your bonds. There must be a torch on the east wall of the dungeon as you can see its light flickering on the ceiling and between the bodies of the Xixon guards around you.

The Xixon officer yells out, "Where issss that jailer? He is sssuppossssed to be here to lock the prissssoner in the ccccell!"

He points to one of the warriors and hisses out an order in his own sibilant tongue, saying the word (or name) "Link". The warrior runs up the stairs leading from the dungeons, you assume in search of the jailer, whose name you guess is "Link".

> x floor
The dungeon floor is made of large flagstones that are covered with a thin layer of filth and slime. Running down the centre is a drainage channel.

> x channel
This just a U-shaped channel which channels water along to a drain somewhere on the floor of the dungeon, but you cannot see it from your present position. You notice a small crevice next to the channel right near where you lay.

The Xixon officer starts speaking to his men and from his gestures towards you and the cells you assume he is giving them orders to guard you.

> x crevice
A crevice about 10 cm wide and 4 cm deep where the edge of a flagstone next to the drainage channel has broken away.

> get goggles
(from the leather pouch)
Moving slowly so as not to alert the Xixon guards, you manage to take the pair of goggles from the leather pouch without fumbling too much with your tied hands.

Suddenly you hear a bell being rung and a Xixon warrior appears on the stairs and shouts something to the officer. Something seems to be going on in the castle above as the officer tells all but two of the warriors to go with the other one. They run up the stairs leaving just the officer and two warriors to guard you.

> hide goggles in crevice
Carefully so as not to alert your guards, you hide the pair of goggles inside the crevice by the drainage channel.

The Xixon warrior returns pushing a squat, heavily-built black man in front of him.

"Alright, alright, keep yer 'air on...if ya 'ad any!" he complains. "Can't a man go to the karzi when he needs to?!".

The Xixon officer points to one of the cells. "Get zzzat door open quickly!" he hisses at the man, who is apparently the jailer. "I can't open number 4," Link sheepishly tells the Xixon. "I..er..lost the key!"

"Zzzen open one of the other doors, any one will do!" the officer rages at Link. He fumbles at a bunch of keys hanging from his belt and, selecting one, unlocks the cell door and pulls it open.

The remaining Xixon warriors haul you to your feet and go to throw you in the cell, but the officer stops them. He draws a large knife and cuts your bonds, and turning to the jailer he hisses, "Make sssure he isss sssecurely ssshackled!"

The Xixon throw you headlong into the cell, where you hit the rear wall with such force that you are momentarily stunned. The warriors grab your arms in a vice-like grip and they roughly pull the chainmail hauberk off you. The jailer Link locks shackles around your wrists then he rummages in your pouch for whatever he can find in there.

They all exit the cell, leaving you in a crumpled heap on the straw-covered floor. The jailer locks the door and stands outside, looking in at you through a small barred window.

"No point me feeding ya," he mutters to himself. "They'll be taking you for the chop soon enough, ya poor sod." He shakes his head and disappears from view.

In Dungeon Cell 1
You are in a small cell in the dungeons of Domreil Castle. The door that is the only exit from the cell leads North and is closed. The only comfort is a pile of dirty straw on the stone floor and the sanitary facility is a latrine hole in the corner. You are shackled with manacles which are attached to chains which hang from ringbolts set into the rear wall of the cell.

As you sit there contemplating your situation, your stomach grumbles complainingly to remind you that you have not eaten anything for a long time!

You get to your feet and stretch, as far as you are able to with these chains impeding you, to get the cramp out of your muscles - what the hell are you going to do now?

"'Ungry are ya? Well... I don't suppose I can begrudge a condemned man a morsel of grub. 'Ang on, I'll be back in a minute."

His face disappears from the window and you guess he has gone to get you some food.

> z

> z

> z

You hear footsteps approach the cell and keys clinkering - it must be Link returning.

The door opens and you see Link the jailer standing there, holding a trencher of food. Behind him stand two Xixon guards to make sure you don't try anything. He bends down and places the trencher on the floor of the cell.

"'Ere ya go, this was all I could rustle up," he says with a snigger. "It'er probably make yer sick, but don't you go moaning at me."

He backs out of the cell and locks the door. His face appears at the grille and he smirks. "No use wasting good food on a condemned man!" His face disappears and you hear him and the Xixon warriors walk away.

By Door in the Linen Room
This large room is where the castle's stock of linen is stored. It is a long, clean, tidy room lined with lots of cupboards from floor to ceiling. In one corner just here there is a desk and chair where the linen mistress would attend to her ledgers. The door leads South to the corridor and you can go West to the other end of the room.  Also here is a wooden chair.  At the west end of the room a woman cowers in the corner aiming a loaded crossbow directly at you.

"Come any closer and I will fire this," the woman warns you with a snarl. "Don't think I won't - I know how to use it!"

> introduce yourself to woman
You talk gently to the woman in an effort to calm her down, telling her who you are, how you got here and what you are doing here.

She eventually lowers the crossbow, uncocking it so that it is safe. She tells you her name is Jasmine and that she is a healer.

"I'm sorry for threatening you with the crossbow," she tells you. "The jailer and a couple of his cronies had tried to get in here to rape me. I shot and wounded one of them and they haven't been back since. I'm too scared to try to get back to my own room as the Xixon will probably catch me before I get to the stairs."

She sees your wounded leg and she tells you to come and sit on the bed.

West End of Linen Room
You are at the west end of the linen room. This would appear to be where the linen mistress lived as there is a bed tucked up against the wall here.  Also here is a crossbow.  Jasmine the healer is here.

Jasmine examines the wound on your thigh, tutting as she sees the dirty bandages you wrapped around it.

"You did a good job bandaging it up to staunch the bleeding, but the wound will need to be stitched," she tells you. "If you can get to my room on the second floor, in there you will find my medicine bag. You can't miss it, it is made from canvas and has herbs embroidered on it."

Jasmine hands you a room key. "This is the key to my room, it's the last door on the south side at the east end of the corridor. Bring my bag back here and I will stitch the cut so that you can walk and fight on it if you have to."

> search cupboards
You open some of the cupboards but they are only full of bundles of linen which are of no use to you, so you close them again. As you open one of the cupboard, however, a length of string falls out onto the floor.

West End of Linen Room
You are at the west end of the linen room. This would appear to be where the linen mistress lived as there is a bed tucked up against the wall here.  Also here is a length of strong string and a crossbow.  Jasmine the healer is here.

> e
You move east.

By Door in the Linen Room
This large room is where the castle's stock of linen is stored. It is a long, clean, tidy room lined with lots of cupboards from floor to ceiling. In one corner just here there is a desk and chair where the linen mistress would attend to her ledgers. The door leads South to the corridor and you can go West to the other end of the room.  Also here is a wooden chair.

> x desk
A plain wooden writing desk it has a drawer for quills and ink to be stored.

> open drawer
You open the desk drawer, rummaging around in amongst the quills.

At first you find only more quills and bits of quill, but then - right at the back of the drawer - your fingers find a hard metal object. You take it out and find it is a door key. You limp back up the other end of the room show it to Jasmine, who looks at it in astonishment.

"That's the key to the door of this room that I was looking for earlier," she tells you in amazement. "I swear I searched that drawer thoroughly three times and it was NOT there!"

You laugh as you hand the key to Jasmine. "Make sure you keep it in your pocket this time," you tell her.

> show bottle to jasmine
You show the bottle of acid to Jasmine and tell her that you found it in the jailer's room. She looks at it with a shocked expression on her face as she speaks to you.

"That proves it then," she tells you. "It was rumoured that Link was being cruel to prisoners who were locked up in the cells. They claimed he would drip acid onto their skin to torment them, but nobody believed them."

She shudders and tells you, "Take it away from here, I don't want it anywhere near me!"

> get string
Ok, you pick up the length of strong string.

> ask jasmine for food
You ask Jasmine if she has any food.

"Yes, I have some travel rations I managed to steal from a kitchen," she tells you. "Here, take some and eat them now, you are probably ravenous!"

She gives you some of the travel rations, which you eat gratefully. The food restores your strength quite a lot. You decide to save some for later in case you get hungry again.

> e
You move east.

Also here is a wooden chair.

Lying on the floor of the chamber with its head smashed in is the body of the Xixon guard. An archway goes East to the passageway that leads to the dungeons.  Also here is a large knife, the rusty key, a heavy wooden cudgel and a whetstone.

> get knife

> search xixon

> search xixon

On Spiral Stairway

From here you can peek around the newel to look west along the corridor. Going Up will take you a few more steps to the archway or you can go back Down to the floor below.

> look w

The Xixon guard turns around and starts to walk away from you.

> creep w
You tiptoe up the stairs and creep quietly along the corridor until you are just behind the Xixon guard.....

Middle of Corridor
You are at the middle of the corridor, which stretches away to East and West. There is just one large door to the north here. On the wall opposite the door a burning torch provides light to see by in this dark corridor.  A Xixon guard is here patrolling the corridor.

> strangle xixon
Wrapping the ends of the length of string around the palms of your hands a couple of times, you quickly whip the string over the head of the Xixon and around its throat and, placing your knee in the small of its back, you pull as hard as you can!

The guard drops his sword on the floor of the corridor with a clatter as it struggles against the string that is choking its life from it but you manage to hang on just long enough and eventually the lizardman's body goes limp and you lower it to the ground.

You lean against the wall of the corridor, exhausted from the effort of killing the Xixon and your injured leg has started to hurt again. Maybe you need to replenish your strength.....

Middle of Corridor
You are at the middle of the corridor, which stretches away to East and West. There is just one large door to the north here. On the wall opposite the door a burning torch provides light to see by in this dark corridor.  Lying sprawled on the floor is the body of the Xixon guard you have just dispatched.  Also here is a broadsword.

> get sword
Ok, you pick up the broadsword.

> eat rations
You eat some of the travel rations and they restore your strength quite a bit.

You hear a sibilant hiss and look up to see a Xixon warrior running towards you from the end of the corridor - it must have heard the noise when the Xixon you just killed dropped the broadsword! The Xixon raises its sword as it charges towards you!

You raise your sword to fend off the attack by the Xixon and, strengthened by the rations you ate, manage to fight back and kill your assailant.

Middle of Corridor
You are at the middle of the corridor, which stretches away to East and West. There is just one large door to the north here. On the wall opposite the door a burning torch provides light to see by in this dark corridor.  Lying sprawled on the floor are the bodies of the Xixon warriors you have just killed.  Also here is a longsword.

> search xixon
You quickly search the bodies of the Xixon guards and on one of them you find a large iron key.

Suddenly you hear loud, out-of-tune whistling and the slap of sandaled feet on the stone floor and look around to see who is making the awful noise.

Your mouth drops open in surprise as you see what appears to be the dwarf Grimmelmulkinsson walking towards you! As the dwarf gets nearer, however, you see that it is not Grim, but a dwarf who looks very much like him. The dwarf stops by the bodies of the two Xixon warriors, looks down at them and sighs.

"My, my," the dwarf growls in a gravelly voice. "We have been busy, ain't we!" Before you have a chance to speak he grabs one of the bodies and hoists it on to his shoulder and then grabs the ankles of the other Xixon with his free hand.

As you stand there watching with dumb astonishment, he walks away down the corridor dragging the body behind him. When he gets near the spiral stairway he stops and looks back. "In case you're wondering, these lizards make great eating when they're roasted!" With that he walks down the stairway, the head of the dead Xixon he is dragging behind him making a dull thud on the stone steps as he disappears from view.

Middle of Corridor

> x iron key
A large iron key which has seen much use.

> unlock door
(using the large iron key)

> n
You move north.

Meeting Room
This is a large ordinary room in the castle, the purpose of which might be that of a meeting room of some sort. The only furniture are several large wooden chairs which surround a large, heavy wooden table. The only door leads South to the corridor.  Sitting at the table, facing you, is a man.

The man, who looks like he could be an officer of rank, looks up as you walk in and, as he was expecting his visitor to be one of the Xixon, regards you with astonishment.

"Who the hell are you and how did you get past that guard?" he asks you. "I am Baron Nigel Coris, commander of the King's personal guard."

You tell the Baron who you are and how you got here, shamefully admitting that you found the lost Axe of Kolt and then promptly lost it when you emerged from the tomb in the midst of the Xixon army.

"Good grief!" he exclaims, rising to his feet. "The Xixon war chiefs have being scouring the land looking for the Axe and it was underneath their army all the time! They must have it in the castle somewhere, I would imagine it is under heavy guard."

He thinks for a while, then continues.

"Look, time is short. You try to recover the Axe while I go and try to release some of our soldiers. If you can get the Axe to Kelson he can invoke its powers and every single Xixon warrior will be disabled so we can round the bastards up and regain control of the castle."

He goes to the door and looks out. "OK, the coast is clear out there, I know where our men are being held. Whatever it takes, get that Axe and put it into Kelson's hand, that's all you have to do."

With that, Baron Coris slips out of the room and is gone.

East End of Corridor
You are at the end of a long corridor on the second floor of Domreil castle, by the archway that leads East into the spiral stairway. There is just one door here to the South and you can continue along the corridor to the West. A flickering torch fitted into a sconce on the wall just here provides enough light to see by.

As you approach the east end of the corridor, a Xixon warrior appears in the archway to the west, having come down from the next floor up. It hisses sibilantly, draws a sword from a scabbard and attacks you with it.

You fight back gallantly and the strain on your wounded leg begins to tell after a minute or two.

You have just enough energy, however, to overwhelm the Xixon and, sending its sword spinning from its hand, you dispatch your attacker with a thrust to the throat!

East End of Corridor
You are at the end of a long corridor on the second floor of Domreil castle, by the archway that leads East into the spiral stairway. There is just one door here to the South and you can continue along the corridor to the West. A flickering torch fitted into a sconce on the wall just here provides enough light to see by.  Lying sprawled on the floor is the body of the Xixon guard you have just dispatched.  Also here is an ordinary sword.

You wince as intense pain stabs at the wound in your thigh and a wave of dizziness sweeps over you. As you are flexing your leg to get rid of the pain, you hear a rather out-of-tune humming coming from your left and you look around to see the same dwarf you saw earlier walking towards you from the stairway.

"Hello there," he says cheerily. "Been fighting again I see!" As before the dwarf hoists the body of the dead Xixon onto one shoulder and with the other hand he picks up the discarded sword.

"Where did you come from?" you ask the dwarf.

"Ah," he says with a wink. "Now that's for me to know and you to find out!" The dwarf starts to walk away but stops. Turning round to you he speaks. "By the way, Grim says thanks for the recipe, we shared the partridge pie, it was delicious!"

He resumes walking towards the far end of the corridor and as he starts to walk down the spiral stairway he calls back, "In case you haven't twigged it, I'm Grim's brother, Grommelmulkinsson, otherwise known as Grom. Be seeing you again, no doubt!" He makes his way down the stairs, humming tunelessly as he goes.

West End of Linen Room
You are at the west end of the linen room. This would appear to be where the linen mistress lived as there is a bed tucked up against the wall here.  Also here is a crossbow.  Jasmine the healer is here.

Jasmine sees the bag you are carrying and she takes it from you.

"Lay down on the bed," she tells you. "And I will stitch your wound up."

You do as you are told and Jasmine tends to your wound. You wince as she cuts the old bandage from around your thigh as the blood has dried and stuck to the material. She takes some herbs from her bag and prepares a tincture which she washes the wound out with. As blood begins to flow from the cut, she threads a large curved needle with some thread and - telling you "This won't hurt a bit!" - proceeds to stitch the lips of the wound together.

You have to grit your teeth a few times as she works, but soon the cut on your thigh has been closed. She finishes up by smearing honey on the wound, telling you it will aid healing, and then she puts a new clean bandage around your thigh.

You get to your feet and test the leg - there is hardly any pain at all and you feel confident that you will be able to complete your quest.

"I've done all I can for you, Alaric," Jasmine tells you. "It is up to you now to find that Axe and get it into the hands of King Kelson."

She gives you a good-luck kiss on the cheek and ushers you out of the room, telling you that she won't answer the door to anyone until you have succeeded in your quest.....

Fresh rushes mixed with lavender cover the floor in an attempt to hide the smell. The corridor is south.  Piled on the floor are some blocks of stone.  Also here is a length of strong string, a pair of gloves, a large iron key, a broadsword and a metal key.

> drop block
OK, you drop the stone block on the pile of blocks.

> x blocks
A pile of 3 stone blocks you removed from the embrasure near the second floor of the castle.

> s
You move south.

West End of Corridor
You are at the west end of a long corridor on the second floor of this section of Domreil castle, by the archway that leads West into the spiral stairway. There are doors to the North and South and you can continue along the corridor to the East. On the wall a guttering torch illuminates the corridor just enough to see by.

> w
You move west.

On Spiral Stairway
You are on the spiral stairway which twists Up and Down at the west end of this section of the castle. Just here an archway leads East to the west end of the corridor on the second floor. Opposite the archway there is an embrasure in the wall.

> remove block
You remove one of the blocks from the side of the arrow slit in the embrasure.

> squeeze through gap
You push your body through the gap and, aided by the butter you smeared on the opening, manage to squeeze through. You grab hold of the drainpipe with one hand and then swing yourself over so you are hanging from the drainpipe.

On Drainpipe By Embrasure
You are hanging from a lead drainpipe high on the west side of one of the buildings of Domreil Castle. You can either climb up or down the drainpipe. The embrasure you climbed through to get here is about a metre away to your right, but you would have great difficulty accessing it from here.

> climb up drainpipe
You climb up the lead drainpipe until you are just below the battlement crenelations. Your leg gives you a bit of pain but the stitching done by Jasmine stops the cut opening again.

At Top of Drainpipe
You are hanging from the top of the lead drainpipe just below the battlements of this part of the castle. You can climb onto the battlements through one of the crenelations just above you.

As you reach the top of the drainpipe, you hear the sibilant speech of a Xixon coming from above you. Pressing yourself against the pipe you look up and see the back of a Xixon warrior above the crenelations about a metre above you. It seems to be talking to another Xixon warrior.

> look up
You look up and see the figure of a Xixon warrior silhouetted against the sky. It is leaning against the battlement crenelations about a metre above you. The creature's back is towards you and you can hear that it is talking to another Xixon in their sibilant, hissing speech.

> x xixon
A Xixon warrior leaning against the crenelations above you with its back towards you. It is wearing a war harness, the straps of which cross over the creature's back.

You hear the Xixon warriors stop talking and footsteps as one of the Xixon warriors walks away. Looking up you see that the Xixon warrior above you is still standing against the crenelations with his back to you.

> grab xixon
You reach up and grab the Xixon warrior by his harness.

You pull the creature over the crenelations and let it drop to the courtyard below. The Xixon hits the hard stones of the courtyard with a sickening thud as its neck snaps, killing it instantly.

> climb over battlements
You grab hold of the crenelations above you and pull yourself over them onto the battlements.....

West End of Battlements
You are at the west end of the battlements of this part of Domreil castle. The battlements extend East and the nearest feature is what appears to be a guardhouse to the SE. Just here is a spiral stairway going Down.

You see a Xixon warrior over by the crenelations further to the east, it seems to be watching something that is going on below. It has its back to you and is unaware of your presence.

> se
You move southeast.

By Side of Guardhouse
You are standing by the side of the guardhouse on the battlements. You can go North or NW from here. Jutting out from the wall of the guardhouse about a metre or so above your head is an iron bar.

The Xixon warrior is still over by the crenelations, now to your north. You had better deal with it quickly before it spots you!

> get knife
(from the large sheath)
Ok, you take the large knife from the large sheath.

> throw knife at xixon
Gripping the knife by the tip of the blade, you draw your arm back over your shoulder and let fly.....

The knife hits the Xixon warrior at the base of its head, severing its spinal cord and killing it instantly. The creature drops like a stone to the ground and lays still.

> grab bar
You jump up and grab hold of the iron bar. It gives a bit under your weight - if you did that a couple more times you might break the bar free from the wall.

> grab bar
You jump up and grab hold of the iron bar. It gives a bit under your weight - if you did that a couple more times you might break the bar free from the wall.

> grab bar
You jump up and grab hold of the iron bar. It gives a bit under your weight - if you did that a couple more times you might break the bar free from the wall.

Suddenly the bar breaks where it is cemented into the wall and you drop to the floor of the battlements, the iron bar in your hand.

> n
You move north.

Near West End of Battlements
You are near the west end of the battlements which extend from East to West. To the South is the guardhouse.  A dead xixon is here.

As you stand there looking down at the Xixon you just killed, you hear soft footsteps behind you and you whip around to see who is creeping up behind you.

A sigh of relief escapes you as you see it is the squat figure of the dwarf Grommelmulkinson walking nonchalantly towards you.

"Sorry if I scared you," he says apologetically. "I heard the noise and thought that you were probably up to your tricks again!"

He reaches down and plucks your knife out of the Xixon's neck and wipes the green blood off on the Xixon's back. He hands the knife to you and then he looks at the boots that the Xixon warrior is wearing and then at your well-worn pair.

"You might as well have these," he says pulling the boots off the Xixon's feet and handing them to you. "This chap has no need of them any more."

As you pull your boots off and replace them with the ones Grom has given you - they fit you like a pair of gloves - the Dwarf bends down to hoist the dead body onto his shoulder. He also picks up your old discarded boots and shoves them on to the feet of the dead lizardman. He puts them on the wrong feet but you think to yourself that the dead Xixon won't really care any more.

"You seem to have stirred up a hornet's nest down below," he warns you. "If you're gonna recover the Axe you'd better hurry up before they realise you are up here. The Axe is in the room below these battlements and young Kelson is incarcerated in the part of the castle to the west of this one."

You thank Grom for the information and watch agape as the dwarf walks to the battlements on the south side, climbs over them with the body over his shoulder and just drops out of view!

> e
You move east.

Middle of Battlements
You are roughly at the middle of the battlements on top of the castle. To the South is the guardhouse and you can go either East or West along the battlements.

> e
You move east.

Near East End of Battlements
You are between the guardhouse and the east end of the battlements. Beyond the crenelations here you see a flagpole jutting out from the wall of the castle. The battlements extend East and West.

> x flagpole
An old wooden flagpole about 3 metres long.  Attached to the flagpole is a lanyard.

> cut lanyard with knife
You reach down and cut the lanyard from the flagpole.

> put knife back
You replace the large knife in the sheath on your belt.

> tie rope to bar
You tie one end of the rope around the middle of the iron bar.

> w
You move west.

Middle of Battlements
You are roughly at the middle of the battlements on top of the castle. To the South is the guardhouse and you can go either East or West along the battlements.

> look d
You look over the battlements and down at the side of the castle below you.  You look down and see a narrow crumbling ledge about 4 metres below the crenelations and what appears to be an iron grille just above it.

> wedge bar behind battlements
You wedge the iron bar behind two of the battlement merlons and throw the rope over the crenelations so that it hangs down the wall below.

> climb down rope
You climb over the battlements and grab hold of the rope. You then slide down the rope until your feet touch the ledge.....

On Ledge by Square Opening
You are standing precariously on a narrow crumbling ledge on the outside wall of the castle. Just here is a square opening in the wall.  An iron grille, firmly cemented into the wall, covers the opening.  A rope hangs down from the battlements above.

> look into opening
You look into the opening and see a brightly lit room with the Axe of Kolt fixed to one of the walls.

> get bottle
(from the leather pouch)
You take the small bottle from the leather pouch.

> pour acid on bars
You unstopper the bottle and carefully pour a little acid onto the bars of the grille where they are cemented into the wall.

There is a hissing sound and acrid smoke as the acid eats into the iron. You slip your arm through the bars to hold the grille before you pour acid onto the last bar holding the grille to the wall. Then you replace the stopper in the bottle.

On Ledge by Square Opening
You are standing precariously on a narrow crumbling ledge on the outside wall of the castle. Just here is a square opening in the wall.  A rope hangs down from the battlements above.

> tie rope to grille
You pull the rope up and tie the end to the iron grille. You then lower the grille until it is dangling from the end of the rope below you.

> put bottle in pouch
You put the small bottle in the pouch.

> climb through opening
You climb through the opening in the wall.

In Empty Room
You are in a small room with a door leading South. On either side of the door and on one of the other walls torches in sconces blaze away, bathing the room in light. On one of the side walls, secured to it with thick steel staples, is the Axe of Kolt.

> get bottle
(from the leather pouch)
You take the small bottle from the leather pouch.

> pour acid on staples
You unstopper the bottle and carefully pour the rest of the acid onto the staples holding the Axe against the wall.

As before there is a hissing sound and acrid smoke as the acid eats into the iron. As you melt the last staple the Axe falls away from the wall and you grip the shaft to stop it falling on the floor and alerting the guards outside. You put the stopper back in the bottle and, as it is now empty, you drop the bottle on the floor.

In Empty Room
You are in a small room with a door leading South. On either side of the door and on one of the other walls torches in sconces blaze away, bathing the room in light.   Also here is a small bottle.

> wear axe
You put the strap over your shoulder so you can carry the Axe of Kolt more easily.

> climb through opening
You climb through the opening onto the ledge outside.....

On Ledge by Square Opening
You are standing precariously on a narrow crumbling ledge on the outside wall of the castle. Just here is a square opening in the wall.  A rope hangs down from the battlements above.

> climb up rope
You climb up the rope and over the crenelations onto the battlements.....

Middle of Battlements
You are roughly at the middle of the battlements on top of the castle. To the South is the guardhouse and you can go either East or West along the battlements.  Wedged behind the crenelations is an iron bar with a rope tied to it that hangs down below.

> pull rope
You pick up the iron bar and pull the rope up from where it is hanging down the wall, being careful not to bang the grille against the wall. You lift the grille over the crenelations and put it down quietly on the battlements and untie the rope from it.

> w
You move west.

Near West End of Battlements
You are near the west end of the battlements which extend from East to West. To the South is the guardhouse.

> w
You move west.

West End of Battlements
You are at the west end of the battlements of this part of Domreil castle. The battlements extend East and the nearest feature is what appears to be a guardhouse to the SE. Just here is a spiral stairway going Down.

> look d
You look over the battlements and down at the side of the castle below you.  You see a drainpipe similar to the one you climbed up running down the side of the castle about three metres directly below you. The top end has broken away, but the rest of it runs down the wall close to the roof of the part of the castle below you.  You can also see the main castle courtyard where a wooden scaffold has been erected. On the scaffold is the ominous sight of a headsman's block.

> e
You move east.

Near West End of Battlements
You are near the west end of the battlements which extend from East to West. To the South is the guardhouse.

> wedge bar behind battlements
You wedge the iron bar behind two of the battlement merlons and throw the rope over the crenelations so that it hangs down the wall below.

> climb down rope
You climb over the battlements and grab hold of the rope. You then slide down the rope as far as you can go.....

Hanging on Rope
You are hanging on the end of the rope about 5 metres below the battlements with your feet against the wall of the castle. About 10 metres below you is the roof of the building jutting out from the main castle There is a drainpipe running down the wall about 2 metres to your right, passing close to the roof down below.  A rope hangs down from the battlements above.

> swing on rope
Using your feet to propel yourself, you jump across the wall of the castle until you are near enough to grab hold of and climb onto the drainpipe.

Clinging to Drainpipe
You are clinging to the drainpipe on the side of the castle. The drainpipe continues up a couple of metres but the upper section has broken away. You can only climb down the drainpipe to the roof top below you from here.

> flick rope
You raise the hand holding the end of the rope and bring it down sharply, flicking the rope.

You have to do this a couple of times but eventually the bar above is loose enough to pull over the battlements through the crenel. As the bar falls you you pull the rope towards you and just manage to grab the bar as it falls past you. You coil the rope around your shoulder so that you are able to free both hands to hold onto the drainpipe.

Clinging to Drainpipe
You are clinging to the drainpipe on the side of the castle. The drainpipe continues up a couple of metres but the upper section has broken away. You can only climb down the drainpipe to the roof top below you from here.

> climb down drainpipe
You clamber down the drainpipe onto the roof of the building below....

Top End of Roof
You are at the upper end of the roof, which slopes Down to the North. The lower end of the roof is about 4 metres away and to the NW there is the rooftop of another building the same distance away. Just here is a drainpipe which runs up the side of the wall of the castle. Beyond the roof in the courtyard, the Xixon are herding the surviving citizens of Domreil into the courtyard to witness the execution of their king.

> d
You move down.

Bottom End of Roof
You are at the bottom of the roof top, about 6 metres above the courtyard which is to the north of you. You can go Up to the top end of the roof top or climb down the drainpipe into the courtyard. The roof top of the building nearest to you is about 4 metres to the northwest. You have a grandstand view of the courtyard from here, where the Xixon are herding the surviving citizens of Domreil into the courtyard to witness the execution of their king.

> look down
You look down from the roof and see that the roof adjacent to this one is about 4 metres away.  You can also see, at a barred window a few metres below the roof of the small building next door, a young man looking through the bars at the scene in the courtyard - it must be King Kelson!

> remove axe
You take the strap off your shoulder and hold the Axe of Kolt in your hand.

You hear a loud sibilant screech and you look around to see who made it - a Xixon archer in the courtyard below has spotted you on the roof. He nocks a war arrow to his bow and aims it at you!

The war arrow fired by the Xixon whizzes past you, shattering into pieces on the wall behind you! Phew, that was close - you might not be so lucky next time.

> shout to kelson
You shout at King Kelson. At first he doesn't hear you but then he looks up at you. However, he doesn't seem to grasp what you are doing on the roof top.

> wave axe
You wave the Axe of Kolt above your head so that Kelson can see it. A look of astonishment appears on his face as he realises what you are showing him.

"Hurry man!" he calls out to you, thrusting his arm through the bars covering the window. "You must give me the Axe - quickly!"

A Xixon in the courtyard below throws a small hand axe at you. The creature's aim is bad and the axe misses you by about a metre!

> u
You move up.

Top End of Roof
You are at the upper end of the roof, which slopes Down to the North. The lower end of the roof is about 4 metres away and to the NW there is the rooftop of another building the same distance away. Just here is a drainpipe which runs up the side of the wall of the castle. Beyond the roof in the courtyard, the Xixon are herding the surviving citizens of Domreil into the courtyard to witness the execution of their king.

> run down
You run down the roof towards the edge...

...and leap across the gap onto the other roof.....

Roof of Building
You are on the roof of the building that juts out from the castle buildings to the northwest of the building you jumped from. All around you in the courtyard below, the surviving citizens of Domreil are being herded into the courtyard to witness the execution of their king.

High above you Xixon warriors have reached the battlements and one of them throws a spear at you! Luckily for you its aim is wild and the spear clatters against the tiles of the roof a couple of metres away! An archer a bit further along the battlements tries its luck and fires a war arrow at you!

The arrow misses your left leg by millimetres! Its flight takes it down into the courtyard where it hits another Xixon warrior in the chest. The creature screeches in agony and then falls lifeless to the ground.

You were lucky again - next time it might be you lying dead on the ground!

> look down
You look down and see King Kelson's right arm protruding from between the bars covering the window of the room he is in below you.

> untie rope
You untie the rope from where it is tied around the iron bar, keeping hold of the rope and dropping the iron bar on the floor beside you.

Some Xixon archers in the courtyard below start to fire arrows at you. They all miss but it is only a matter of time before one of them hits you!

> tie rope to axe
You tie one end of the rope around the head of the Axe of Kolt.

> lower axe
You quickly lower the Axe down until it is next to Kelson's outstretched hand, which grabs the weapon and waves it in triumph! Kelson fumbles as he unties it from the rope but then the Axe disappears from view.

Suddenly you start to hear a loud humming sound emanating from the building below you where Kelson is incarcerated.

Press Any Key to Continue.....

You hear sibilant screams and cries of pain and look out at the courtyard in disbelief. All around, Xixon warriors are staggering about or writhing on the ground, holding their hands over their ears. Some lay still on the ground, already dead.

At first the humans in the courtyard are too surprised to do anything, but once they realise that the Xixon are incapacitated, the citizens of Domreil leap upon the lizardmen, seizing their weapons and turning them on their erstwhile captors.

Baron Coris soon arrives with the soldiers he has freed from the dungeons and King Kelson is liberated from his prison. Everywhere he goes with the Axe the Xixon fall like ninepins and the few that survive are easily dealt with.

Over the next few days you start to recover from the wounds you received in and on the castle, closely tended by Jasmine, who uses her skills as a healer to tend your hurts.

Several days later when you are able to walk, with order restored to Domreil castle, you are summoned into the King's audience chamber.....

Press Enter to Continue.....

The High Officials of Hecate and Magor the Sorcerer are present as King Kelson personally thanks you for your bravery and resourcefulness in finding the lost "Axe of Kolt" and getting it into his hand so that the Xixon can be overcome once again.

As a reward for your exploits, he raises you to the rank of Duke and gives you the Duchy of Charlton as a reward. You are honoured by this and on bended knee you vow to be the King's liege man hereafter.

* * * * * * * * * *

You have Completed the Quest to Find...

THE AXE OF KOLT

In 1170 turns, scoring a total of 1187 points!
